/*           TRKCELL=, VOLUME=                                      */

/*TOSC1,D=T; TOSC2,D=T; TOSC3,D=T; TOSC4,D=T           */

./ ADD NAME=LNKLNK   0100-00148-00148-1048-01324-01324-00000-GERHARD
LNK      TITLE  'LNKLNK (RELAY) - LINKAGE MANAGEMENT'
***********************************************************************
*                                                                     *
*                             L N K L N K                             *
*                                                                     *
*---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*                                                                     *
*  COPYRIGHT INFORMATION -                                            *
*                                                                     *
*        COPYRIGHT (C) RELAY TECHNOLOGY, INC.  1995                   *
*            ALL RIGHTS RESERVED                                      *
*                                                                     *
*  MODULE NAME -                                                      *
*                                                                     *
*        LNKLNK                                                       *
*                                                                     *
*  FUNCTION -                                                         *
*                                                                     *
*        LINKAGE MANAGEMENT ROUTINES FOR THE RELAY SYSTEM             *
*                                                                     *
*  ATTRIBUTES -                                                       *
*                                                                     *
*        RESIDENT, REENTERANT                                         *
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY POINTS -                                                     *
*                                                                     *
*        LNKLNKIN - LINKAGE INITIALIZATION                            *
*        LNKLNKAT - CREATE A SUBTASK                                  *
*        LNKLNKDT - DELETE A SUBTASK                                  *
*        LNKLNKDF - HANDLE "DEFER" TYPE LINKAGE                       *
*        LNKLNKLK - HANDLE "LINK" TYPE LINKAGE                        *
*        LNKLNKRT - HANDLE LINKAGE RETURN                             *
*        LNKLNKSA - ALLOCATE A NEW SAVE AREA                          *
*        LNKLNKSR - RETURN THE CURRENT SAVE AREA                      *
*        LNKLNKXC - HANDLE "XCTL" TYPE LINKAGE                        *
*        LNKLNKTR - LINKAGE TERMINATION                               *
*                                                                     *
*  ABENDS -                                                           *
*                                                                     *
*        LNK001 - ATTEMPT TO "CALL" A NONEXISTANT ROUTINE.            *
*        LNK002 - INVALID "RETURN" LINKAGE USED.                      *
*        LNK003 - ATTEMPT TO "XCTL" A NONEXISTANT ROUTINE.            *
*        LNK004 - ATTEMPT TO "DEFER" A NONEXISTANT ROUTINE.           *
*        LNK005 - ATTEMPT TO "DEFER" WITHOUT A LINE BLOCK.            *
*                                                                     *
*  NOTES -                                                            *
*                                                                     *
*        1. THIS MODULE PROVIDES SERVICES USED FOR LINKING            *
*           BETWEEN ROUTINES IN THE SYSTEM. FOR MORE INFORMATION,     *
*           REFER TO THE INDIVIDUAL ENTRY POINTS CONTAINED IN         *
*           THIS MODULE.                                              *
*                                                                     *
***********************************************************************
         EJECT
         COPY   GLOBALS           GLOBAL DEFINITIONS:
         EJECT
***********************************************************************
*                                                                     *
*                          MODULE DEFINITION                          *
*                                                                     *
***********************************************************************
         SPACE  2
LNKLNK   BEGIN  BASE=R12          BEGIN OF MODULE:
         USING  SAVEAREA,R13      SAVE AREA ADDRESSABILITY
         USING  MASTER,R10        MASTER CONTROL BLOCK ADDRESSABILITY
         USING  LINE,R8           LINE CONTROL BLOCK ADDRESSABILITY
         EJECT ,                                               M0019RLY
         AIF (&S$CMS OR &S$TSO).AT001                          M0019RLY
***********************************************************************
*                                                                     *
*                           L N K L N K A T                           *
*                                                                     *
*---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY POINT NAME -                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*        LNKLNKAT                                                     *
*                                                                     *
*  FUNCTION -                                                         *
*                                                                     *
*        PERFORM THE CREATION OF A SUBTASK.                           *
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY CONDITIONS -                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*        R1  = ADDRESS OF THE PARAM LIST PASSED TO THE SUBTASK        *
*              (SUBTASK LINE CONTROL BLOCK)                           *
*        R2  = ADDRESS OF THE SUBTASK TERMINATION EXIT                *
*        R3  = ADDRESS OF THE ABEND EXIT ROUTINE                      *
*        R8  = ADDRESS OF THE LINE BLOCK (CALLEE)                     *
*        R10 = ADDRESS OF THE MASTER CONTROL BLOCK                    *
*        R14 = CALLER'S RETURN ADDRESS                                *
*        R15 = ENTRY POINT ADDRESS, =A(LNKLNKAT)                      *
*                                                                     *
*  EXIT CONDITIONS -                                                  *
*                                                                     *
*        R1  =   ADDRESS OF THE TCB FOR SUBTASK IDENTIFICATION        *
*        R15 =   RETURN CODE                                          *
*                                                                     *
*  REGISTER USAGE -                                                   *
*                                                                     *
*        R15   = ADDRESS FOR SUBTASK ENTRY POINT NAME                 *
*        R14   = RETURN ADDRESS FOR LINKAGE                           *
*        R13   = UNUSED                                               *
*        R12   = MODULE BASE ADDRESS                                  *
*        R11   = UNUSED                                               *
*        R10   = ADDRESS OF THE MASTER CONTROL BLOCK                  *
*        R9    = WORK                                                 *
*        R8    = ADDRESS OF THE LINE BLOCK (CALLEE)                   *
*        R7-R2 = WORK                                                 *
*        R1    = ENTRY/EXIT ADDRESSES (ECB & TCB)                     *
*        R0    = WORK                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*  NOTES -                                                            *
*                                                                     *
*        1. THIS SUBROUTINE IS RESPONSIBLE FOR CREATING A SUBTASK     *
*           VIA 'ATTACH' PROCESSING. THE 'CREATING' TASK WILL BE      *
*           NOTIFIED OF THE SUBTASK'S ENDING VIA AN EXIT. THE         *
*           TASK CONTROL BLOCK ADDRESS WILL BE RETURNED AS AN         *
*           IDENTIFIER FOR THE SUBTASK.                               *
*                                                                     *
*        2. THE ADDRESS OF THE NEW ENTRY POINT IS DETERMINED          *
*           BY EXECUTING THE INSTRUCTION FOLLOWING THE                *
*           "BAL" TO THIS ROUTINE. THAT IS, THE INSTRUCTION           *
*           AT 0(R14) ON ENTRY HERE. THE EVENTUAL RETURN IS           *
*           MADE TO 4(R14).                                           *
*                                                                     *
*        3. UPON EXIT, REGISTER 1 CONTAINS THE ADDRESS OF             *
*           THE TCB FOR SUBTASK IDENTIFICATION.                       *
*                                                                     *
***********************************************************************
         SPACE  2                                              M0019RLY
LNKLNKAT ENTER  BASE=,SAVE=       CREATE A SUBTASK:            M0019RLY
         EX     0,0(R14)          EXECUTE TO LOCATE CALLEE     M0019RLY
         LA     R14,4(,R14)       AND INCREMENT RETURN ADDRESS M0019RLY
         LA     R15,0(,R15)       PURIFY THE ADDRESS           M0019RLY
         STM    R0,R15,COMSVLNK   SAVE CALLERS REGISTERS       M0019RLY
         L      R13,COMSVFRE      POINT TO A SAVE AREA         M0019RLY
         L      R12,MSTLKBAS      LOAD MODULE BASE ADDRESS     M0019RLY
         CL     R15,MSTRELOC      CALLEE'S ADDRESS = ZERO?     M0019RLY
         BZ     LNK007            YES - BRANCH (ERROR)         M0019RLY
         SPACE  2                                              M0019RLY
*
*        ATTACH THE ROUTINE.
*
*** R3270 customer reports 22A abends. Dump shows clobbered LINAREA3,
*** as though used by another task. Pending permanent resolution (e.g.,
*** GETMAIN for unique area), will try LINABREG instead.        GP00141
         MVC    LINABREG(ATTCHEND-ATTCHLST),ATTCHLST  MOVE      GP00141
*OLD*    LA     R4,ATTCHEND       CALCULATE LENGTH OF PARM LISTM0019RLY
*OLD*    LA     R5,ATTCHLST       ...                          M0019RLY
*OLD*    SR     R4,R5             ...                          M0019RLY
*OLD*    BCTR   R4,0              SUBT 1 FROM LENGTH FOR EXEC  M0019RLY
*OLD*    EX     R4,LNKATMV        GO MOVE THE PARM LIST TO WORKM0019RLY
         LR     R5,R1             COPY LINE BLOCK ADDRESS      M0019RLY
         LR     R6,R15            COPY EP NAME ADDRESS         M0019RLY
         AIF (&S$MVFT).ATT1                                    M0653RLY
         ATTACH EPLOC=(R6),ETXR=(R2),ESTAI=((R3),(R5)),        M0019RLY+
               PURGE=HALT,TERM=NO,SM=SUPV,                     F0337RLY+
               SF=(E,LINABREG),MF=(E,(R5))                      GP00141
*OLD*          SF=(E,LINAREA3),MF=(E,(R5))                     M0019RLY
         AGO .ATT1A                                            M0653RLY
.ATT1    ANOP  ,                                               M0653RLY
         ATTACH EPLOC=(R6),ETXR=(R2),ESTAI=((R3),(R5)),        M0653RLY+
               PURGE=HALT,TERM=NO,SM=SUPV,SZERO=NO,            M0653RLY+
               JSTCB=YES,SF=(E,LINAREA3),MF=(E,(R5))           M0653RLY
.ATT1A   ANOP  ,                                               M0653RLY
         LTR    R15,R15           ATTACH SUCCESSFUL??          M0019RLY
         BNZ    LNK007            NO ... BRANCH                M0019RLY
         SPACE  2                                              M0019RLY
         AIF    (NOT &SDIAG).ATDIAG1                           M0019RLY
*
*        SAVE DIAGNOSTICS INFORMATION.
*
LNKATCT  CSADD  MSTLKNMA,WK1=R2,WK2=R3  REQUESTS WE PROCESS:   M0019RLY
.ATDIAG1 ANOP  ,                                               M0019RLY
         SPACE  2                                              M0019RLY
*
*        THE TASK HAS BEEN CREATED.
*
         L      R0,COMSVLNK       RESTORE CALLER'S REGISTERS   M0019RLY
         LM     R2,R14,LNKSVR2    ...                          M0019RLY
         SR     R15,R15           CLEAR RETURN CODE            M0019RLY
         BR     R14               - RETURN TO CALLER -         M0019RLY
         SPACE  2                                              M0019RLY
LNKATMV  MVC    LINAREA3(0),ATTCHLST  - EXECUTED -             M0019RLY
         SPACE  2                                              M0019RLY
*
*        FATAL ERROR: UNABLE TO ATTACH NEW SUBTASK.
*
LNK007   PABEND  007              *** INVALID ATTACH ***       M0019RLY
.AT001   ANOP  ,                                               M0019RLY
         EJECT
***********************************************************************
*                                                                     *
*                           L N K L N K D F                           *
*                                                                     *
*---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY POINT NAME -                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*        LNKLNKDF                                                     *
*                                                                     *
*  FUNCTION -                                                         *
*                                                                     *
*        PERFORM "DEFER" TYPE LINKAGE                                 *
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY CONDITIONS -                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*        R8  = ADDRESS OF THE LINE CONTROL BLOCK                      *
*        R10 = ADDRESS OF THE MASTER CONTROL BLOCK                    *
*        R14 = CALLER'S RETURN ADDRESS                                *
*        R15 = ENTRY POINT ADDRESS, =A(LNKLNKDF)                      *
*                                                                     *
*  EXIT CONDITIONS -                                                  *
*                                                                     *
*        R1  = ADDRESS OF THE SAVEAREA QUEUED FOR DISPATCH.           *
*        R15 = ADDRESS OF THE ROUTINE FOR DEFERRED CALL.              *
*                                                                     *
*  REGISTER USAGE -                                                   *
*                                                                     *
*        R15   = ENTRY ADDRESS FOR LINKAGE & WORK                     *
*        R14   = RETURN ADDRESS FOR LINKAGE                           *
*        R13   = UNUSED                                               *
*        R12   = MODULE BASE ADDRESS                                  *
*        R11   = UNUSED                                               *
*        R10   = ADDRESS OF THE MASTER CONTROL BLOCK                  *
*        R9-R0 = WORK                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*  NOTES -                                                            *
*                                                                     *
*        1. THIS SUBROUTINE PROVIDES DEFERRED LINKAGE TO A ROUTINE.   *
*           WE RETURN IMMEDIATELY TO OUR CALLER; THE SPECIFIED        *
*           ROUTINE WILL BE LATER CALLED FROM THE DISPATCHER.         *
*           DEFER TO THE "LNKDSP" MODULE FOR MORE INFORMATION.        *
*                                                                     *
*        2. THE CALLEE'S ADDRESS IS DETERMINED BY EXECUTING THE       *
*           INSTRUCTION JUST AFTER THE "BAL" TO THIS ROUTINE.         *
*           THAT IS, THE INSTRUCTION AT 0(R14) ON ENTRY HERE. THE     *
*           EVENTUAL RETURN IS MADE TO 4(R14).                        *
*                                                                     *
***********************************************************************
         SPACE  2
LNKLNKDF ENTER  BASE=,SAVE=       QUEUE UP TASK FOR DISPATCH:
         SPACE  2
         AIF    (&S$VTAM).DF001                                M0019RLY
*
*        DISPATCH A ROUTINE: FIRST LOAD THE CALLEE'S ADDRESS,
*        UPDATE OUR CALLER'S RETURN ADDRESS, AND SAVE THE
*        CALLER'S REGISTERS (TEMPORARILY). THEN RELOAD OUR
*        MODULE'S BASE REGISTER AND UPDATE VARIOUS LINKAGE
*        STATISTICS.
*
         EX     0,0(R14)          EXECUTE TO LOCATE CALLEE
         LA     R14,4(,R14)       AND INCREMENT RETURN ADDRESS
         LA     R15,0(,R15)       PURIFY CALLEE'S ADDRESS VALUE
         A      R15,MSTRELOC      RELOCATE THE ADDRESS CONSTANT
         STM    R0,R15,COMSVLNK   SAVE CALLER'S REGISTERS HERE M0019RLY
         L      R12,MSTLKBAS      LOAD MODULE BASE ADDRESS
         CL     R15,MSTRELOC      HAD ZERO FOR CALLEE'S ADDRESS?
         BZ     LNK004            YES - CALLEE DOES NOT EXIST
         LTR    R8,R8             DO WE HAVE A LINE BLOCK NOW?
         BZ     LNK005            NO - WE CANNOT DISPATCH WITHOUT
         SPACE
         AIF    (NOT &SDIAG).DFDIAG1                           M0019RLY
         LA     R1,1              LOAD A CONSTANT VALUE
         A      R1,MSTLKNMD       BUMP COUNT OF "DEFER" REQUESTS
         ST     R1,MSTLKNMD       ...
.DFDIAG1 ANOP  ,                                               M0019RLY
         SPACE  2
*
*        ALLOCATE A SAVE AREA AND ADD IT TO THE DISPATCH QUEUE.
*
         BAL    R9,GETSAVE        ALLOCATE A NEW SAVEAREA
         CALL   LNKDSPQU          QUEUE THIS UP FOR DISPATCH
         L      R14,LNKSVR14      LOAD CALLER'S RETURN ADDRESS
         ST     R14,SAVECR14      SAVE THIS FOR DIAGNOSTIC USE
         SPACE  2
*
*        RETURN TO OUR CALLER, FIRST SETTING REGISTERS TO BE
*        PASS TO THE DISPATCHED ROUTINE IN THE SAVEAREA FOR
*        THAT ROUTINE.
*
         LA     R14,LNKLNKRT      POINT TO OUR RETURN ADDRESS
         L      R15,LNKSVR15      LOAD ADDRESS OF THE CALLEE
         AIF    (NOT &SDIAG).DFDIAG2                           M0043RLY
         ST     R15,SAVECR15      SAVE THIS FOR DIAGNOSTIC USE M0043RLY
.DFDIAG2 ANOP   ,                                              M0043RLY
         LM     R0,R12,COMSVLNK   RESTORE REMAINING REGISTERS  M0019RLY
         STM    R14,R12,SAVEREGS  SET REGISTERS IN QUEUED SAVEAREA
         SPACE
         LR     R1,R13            RETURN SAVEAREA ADDRESS IN R1
         LM     R13,R14,LNKSVR13  RESTORE CALLER'S REGISTERS
         BR     R14               - RETURN TO OUR CALLER -
         SPACE  2
*
*        FATAL ERROR: ATTEMPT TO DEFER A NONEXISTANT ROUTINE.
*
LNK004   PABEND 004               *** INVALID DEFER ATTEMPT ***
.DF001   ANOP   ,                                              M0019RLY
         SPACE  2
*
*        FATAL ERROR: ATTEMPT TO DEFER WITHOUT A LINE BLOCK.
*
LNK005   PABEND 005               *** INVALID DEFER ATTEMPT ***
         EJECT ,                                               M0019RLY
         AIF   (&S$CMS OR &S$TSO).DT001                        M0019RLY
***********************************************************************
*                                                                     *
*                           L N K L N K D T                           *
*                                                                     *
*---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY POINT NAME -                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*        LNKLNKDT                                                     *
*                                                                     *
*  FUNCTION -                                                         *
*                                                                     *
*        PERFORM THE DELETION OF A SUBTASK.                           *
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY CONDITIONS -                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*        R1  = ADDRESS OF THE TASK CONTROL BLOCK                      *
*        R8  = ADDRESS OF THE LINE BLOCK (CALLEE)                     *
*        R10 = ADDRESS OF THE MASTER CONTROL BLOCK                    *
*        R14 = CALLER'S RETURN ADDRESS                                *
*        R15 = ENTRY POINT ADDRESS, =A(LNKLNKDT)                      *
*                                                                     *
*  EXIT CONDITIONS -                                                  *
*                                                                     *
*        R15 = 0; THIS IS ALWAYS SUCCESSFUL (CC=0)                    *
*                                                                     *
*  REGISTER USAGE -                                                   *
*                                                                     *
*        R15   = ENTRY ADDRESS FOR LINKAGE & WORK                     *
*        R14   = RETURN ADDRESS FOR LINKAGE                           *
*        R13   = UNUSED                                               *
*        R12   = MODULE BASE ADDRESS                                  *
*        R11   = UNUSED                                               *
*        R10   = ADDRESS OF THE MASTER CONTROL BLOCK                  *
*        R9    = WORK                                                 *
*        R8    = ADDRESS OF THE LINE BLOCK (CALLEE)                   *
*        R7-R2 = WORK                                                 *
*        R1    = ENTRY ADDRESS  (TCB)                                 *
*        R0    = WORK                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*  NOTES -                                                            *
*                                                                     *
*        1. THIS SUBROUTINE IS RESPONSIBLE FOR DELETING A SUBTASK     *
*           VIA 'DETACH' PROCESSING. THE 'DELETING' TASK WILL         *
*           SUPPLY THE TASK CONTROL BLOCK ADDRESS, WHICH              *
*           IDENTIFIES THE APPROPRIATE SUBTASK.                       *
*                                                                     *
*        2. UPON ENTRY, REGISTER 1 CONTAINS THE ADDRESS OF            *
*           THE TCB FOR SUBTASK IDENTIFICATION.                       *
*                                                                     *
***********************************************************************
         SPACE  2                                              M0019RLY
LNKLNKDT ENTER  BASE=,SAVE=       DELETE A SUBTASK:            M0019RLY
         STM    R0,R15,COMSVLNK   SAVE CALLERS REGISTERS       M0019RLY
         L      R12,MSTLKBAS      LOAD MODULE BASE ADDRESS     M0019RLY
         SPACE  2                                              M0019RLY
*
*        DETACH THE ROUTINE.
*
         DETACH (R1),STAE=NO      DETACH THE SUBTASK           M0019RLY
         LTR    R15,R15           REQUEST OK??                 M0019RLY
         BNZ    LNK008            NO ... BRANCH                M0019RLY
         SPACE  2                                              M0019RLY
         AIF    (NOT &SDIAG).DTDIAG1                           M0019RLY
*
*        SAVE DIAGNOSTICS INFORMATION.
*
LNKDTCT  CSADD  MSTLKNMS,WK1=R2,WK2=R3  REQUESTS PROCESSED:    M0019RLY
.DTDIAG1 ANOP  ,                                               M0019RLY
         SPACE  2                                              M0019RLY
*
*        THE TASK HAS BEEN DELETED.
*
         LM     R0,R14,COMSVLNK   RESTORE CALLER'S REGISTERS   M0019RLY
         BR     R14               - RETURN TO CALLER -         M0019RLY
         SPACE  2                                              M0019RLY
*
*        FATAL ERROR: UNABLE TO DETACH THE SUBTASK.
*
LNK008   PABEND 008               *** INVALID DETACH ***       M0019RLY
.DT001   ANOP  ,                                               M0019RLY
         EJECT
***********************************************************************
*                                                                     *
*                           L N K L N K I N                           *
*                                                                     *
*---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY POINT NAME -                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*        LNKLNKIN                                                     *
*                                                                     *
*  FUNCTION -                                                         *
*                                                                     *
*        INITIALIZE THE LINKAGE MANAGER                               *
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY CONDITIONS -                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*        R1  = POINTER TO SUBTASK ENTRY NAME FOR RELAY/3270-VTAM      *
*        R14 = CALLER'S RETURN ADDRESS                                *
*        R15 = ENTRY POINT ADDRESS, =A(LNKLNKIN)                      *
*                                                                     *
*  EXIT CONDITIONS -                                                  *
*                                                                     *
*        R15 = 0; THIS IS ALWAYS SUCCESSFUL (CC=0).                   *
*                                                                     *
*  REGISTER USAGE -                                                   *
*                                                                     *
*        R15   = ENTRY ADDRESS FOR LINKAGE & WORK                     *
*        R14   = RETURN ADDRESS FOR LINKAGE                           *
*        R13   = UNUSED                                               *
*        R12   = MODULE BASE ADDRESS                                  *
*        R11   = UNUSED                                               *
*        R10   = ADDRESS OF THE MASTER CONTROL BLOCK                  *
*        R9-R0 = WORK                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*  NOTES -                                                            *
*                                                                     *
*        1. THIS SUBROUTINE PREALLOCATES A BLOCK OF SAVE AREAS        *
*           USED FOR LATER LINKAGE (THE LOCALIZATION OF STORAGE       *
*           IS A BETTER WAY THAN ALLOCATING ALL AREAS OUT OF FREE     *
*           STORAGE WHEN REQUIRED). THE "PRESAVE" EQUATE (SEE THE     *
*           END OF THIS MODULE) DEFINES THE NUMBER OF AREAS TO BE     *
*           ALLOCATED.                                                *
*                                                                     *
*        2. IF THE "MSTSVARS" AND "MSTSVARE" VALUES ARE SET BEFORE    *
*           CALLING THIS ROUTINE, THE AREA PREVIOUSLY ALLOCATED       *
*           WILL BE USED.                                             *
*                                                                     *
***********************************************************************
         SPACE  2
LNKLNKIN ENTER  SAVE=COMSVLNK     INITIALIZE LINKAGE MANAGEMENTM0019RLY
         LR     R4,R1             SAVE VTAM EP NAME ADDRESS    M0019RLY
         SPACE  2
*
*        SET VARIOUS ROUTINE ADDRESSES IN THE MASTER CONTROL BLOCK.
*
         LA     R0,LNKLNKLK       POINT TO "LINK" PROCESSING ROUTINE
         ST     R0,MSTLKAD1       SET ADDRESS FOR LATER USE
         LA     R0,LNKLNKXC       POINT TO "XCTL" PROCESSING ROUTINE
         ST     R0,MSTLKAD2       SET ADDRESS FOR LATER USE
         LA     R0,LNKLNKDF       POINT TO "DEFER" PROCESSING ROUTINE
         ST     R0,MSTLKAD3       SET ADDRESS FOR LATER USE
         AIF    (&S$CMS OR &S$TSO).IN001                       M0019RLY
         LA     R0,LNKLNKAT       POINT TO "ATTACH" PROCESSING M0019RLY
         ST     R0,MSTLKAD4       SET ADDRESS FOR LATER USE    M0019RLY
         LA     R0,LNKLNKDT       POINT TO "DETACH" PROCESSING M0019RLY
         ST     R0,MSTLKAD5       SET ADDRESS FOR LATER USE    M0019RLY
.IN001   ANOP  ,                                               M0019RLY
         ST     R12,MSTLKBAS      SET MODULE BASE ADDRESS
         SPACE  2
         AIF    (&S$VTAM).IN002                                M0019RLY
*
*        ALLOCATE A BLOCK OF SAVE AREAS FOR LATER LINKAGE.
*        THESE ARE THEN PLACED ON THE FREE SAVEAREA CHAIN.
*
         ICM    R0,15,MSTSVARS         DO WE HAVE SOMETHING ALREADY?
         BNZ    INSAVE1                YES - WE WILL USE THIS AREA
         LA     R0,PRESAVE*SAVESIZE    GET SIZE OF REQUIRED AREA
         LA     R2,ALCZERO+ALABERR     LOAD OPTIONS FOR ALLOCATION
         CALL   LNKSTGAL               GO TO ALLOCATE STORAGE AREA
         STM    R0,R1,MSTSVARS         SAVE AREA SIZE & ADDRESS
         SPACE
INSAVE1  EQU    *                      LINK TOGETHER FREE SAVEAREAS:
         L      R13,MSTSVARE           LOAD POINTER TO AREA BEGIN
         SRDL   R0,32                  SHIFT DOWN SIZE OF STORAGE
         D      R0,=A(SAVESIZE)        GET NUMBER OF SAVEAREAS HERE
         LR     R0,R1                  COPY COUNT VALUE FOR LOOP
         SR     R1,R1                  CLEAR INITIAL FORWARD POINTER
         SPACE
INLOOP1  EQU    *                      LOOP TO CHAIN THE AREAS:
         ST     R1,SAVELINK            SET FORWARD POINTER IN SAVEAREA
         LR     R1,R13                 COPY ADDRESS OF THIS AREA
         LA     R13,SAVEALEN(,R13)     POINT UP TO THE NEXT AREA
         BCT    R0,INLOOP1             - LOOP TO CHAIN AREAS -
         SPACE
         ST     R1,COMSVFRE            SET LAST AREA AT FRONT OM0019RLY
         SPACE  2                                              M0019RLY
*
*        LINKAGE INITIALIZATION IS NOW COMPLETE.
*
         RETURN RC=0,SAVE=COMSVLNK     - RETURN TO OUR CALLER -M0019RLY
         AGO    .IN003                                         M0019RLY
.IN002   ANOP  ,                                               M0019RLY
*
*        CREATE AN ENTRY POINT NAME FOR SUBTASK CREATION.
*
         L      R1,MSTSUBTA       POINT TO SUBTASK START ADDR  M0019RLY
         LR     R0,R4             COPY THE EP NAME ADDRESS     M0019RLY
         IDENTIFY EPLOC=((R0)),   CREATE THE ENTRY POINT       M0019RLY+
               ENTRY=((R1))       ...                          M0019RLY
         LTR    R15,R15           RETURN CODE = 0??            M0019RLY
         BNZ    LNK006            NO ... BRANCH                M0019RLY
         SPACE  2                                              M0019RLY
*
*        LINKAGE INITIALIZATION IS NOW COMPLETE.
*
         RETURN RC=0,SAVE=COMSVLNK     - RETURN TO OUR CALLER -M0019RLY
         SPACE  2                                              M0019RLY
*
*        FATAL ERROR: CANNOT CREATE ENTRY POINT
*
LNK006   PABEND 006               *** CANNOT CREATE E.P. ***   M0019RLY
.IN003   ANOP   ,                                              M0019RLY
         EJECT
***********************************************************************
*                                                                     *
*                           L N K L N K L K                           *
*                                                                     *
*---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY POINT NAME -                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*        LNKLNKLK                                                     *
*                                                                     *
*  FUNCTION -                                                         *
*                                                                     *
*        PERFORM "LINK" TYPE LINKAGE                                  *
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY CONDITIONS -                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*        R8  = ADDRESS OF THE LINE BLOCK, IF PRESENT                  *
*        R10 = ADDRESS OF THE MASTER CONTROL BLOCK                    *
*        R14 = CALLER'S RETURN ADDRESS                                *
*        R15 = ENTRY POINT ADDRESS, =A(LNKLNKLK)                      *
*                                                                     *
*  EXIT CONDITIONS -                                                  *
*                                                                     *
*        EXIT VIA BRANCH TO CALLEE ROUTINE (SEE NOTES BELOW).         *
*                                                                     *
*  REGISTER USAGE -                                                   *
*                                                                     *
*        R15   = ENTRY ADDRESS FOR LINKAGE & WORK                     *
*        R14   = RETURN ADDRESS FOR LINKAGE                           *
*        R13   = UNUSED                                               *
*        R12   = MODULE BASE ADDRESS                                  *
*        R11   = UNUSED                                               *
*        R10   = ADDRESS OF THE MASTER CONTROL BLOCK                  *
*        R9-R0 = WORK                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*  NOTES -                                                            *
*        1. THIS SUBROUTINE PROVIDES CALL-AND-RETURN TYPE LINKAGE     *
*           BETWEEN TWO ROUTINES (TERMED THE CALLER AND THE CALLEE).  *
*           A SAVE AREA FOR USE BY THE CALLEE IS ALLOCATED AND THE    *
*           ENTRY POINT ADDRESS IS RELOCATED.                         *
*                                                                     *
*        2. THE CALLEE'S ADDRESS IS DETERMINED BY EXECUTING THE       *
*           INSTRUCTION JUST AFTER THE "BAL" TO THIS ROUTINE.         *
*           THAT IS, THE INSTRUCTION AT 0(R14) ON ENTRY HERE. THE     *
*           EVENTUAL RETURN IS MADE TO 4(R14).                        *
*                                                                     *
*        3. ON ENTRY TO THE CALLED ROUTINE, R13 POINTS TO A SAVE      *
*           AREA AVAILABLE FOR USE, R14 POINTS TO "LNKLNKRT" (WHICH   *
*           HANDLES ALL RETURN PROCESSING), AND R15 CONTAINS THE      *
*           ENTRY POINT ADDRESS. ALL OTHER REGISTERS HAVE THEIR       *
*           CONTENTS UNCHANGED FROM THE CALL TO THIS ROUTINE. IT      *
*           IS THE CALLEE'S RESPONSIBILITY TO PRESERVE AND LATER      *
*           RESTORE THE REGISTERS PASSED THERE.                       *
*                                                                     *
***********************************************************************
         EJECT
***********************************************************************
*                                                                     *
*                           L N K L N K L K                           *
*                                                                     *
*---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*                                                                     *
*  NOTES -                                                            *
*                                                                     *
*        4. ALSO REFER TO THE "LNKLNKXC" ROUTINE FOR ADDITIONAL       *
*           INFORMATION.                                              *
*                                                                     *
***********************************************************************
         SPACE  2
LNKLNKLK ENTER  BASE=,SAVE=            LINK TO ANOTHER ROUTINE:
         SPACE  2
*
*        CALL A SUBROUTINE: FIRST LOAD THE CALLEE'S ADDRESS,
*        UPDATE OUR CALLER'S RETURN ADDRESS, AND SAVE THE
*        CALLER'S REGISTERS (TEMPORARILY). THEN RELOAD OUR
*        MODULE'S BASE REGISTER AND UPDATE VARIOUS LINKAGE
*        STATISTICS.
*
         EX     0,0(R14)          EXECUTE TO LOCATE CALLEE
         LA     R14,4(,R14)       AND INCREMENT RETURN ADDRESS
         AL     R15,MSTRELOC      RELOCATE THE ADDRESS CONSTANT
         STM    R0,R15,COMSVLNK   SAVE CALLER'S REGISTERS HERE M0019RLY
         L      R12,MSTLKBAS      LOAD MODULE BASE ADDRESS     M0019RLY
         LA     R15,0(,R15)       PURIFY CALLEE'S ADDRESS VALUE
         CL     R15,MSTRELOC      HAD ZERO FOR CALLEE'S ADDRESSM0019RLY
         BZ     LNK001            YES - CALLEE DOES NOT EXIST  M0019RLY
         ICM    R2,15,LNKSVR12    CHECK CALLER'S R12           M0339RLY
         BZ     LNK001            ZERO - LINKAGE ERROR         M0339RLY
         SPACE  2                                              M0019RLY
         AIF    (NOT &SDIAG).LKCNT1B                           M0019RLY
*
*        SAVE DIAGNOSTIC INFORMATION
*
LKCOUNTS CSADD  MSTLKNMC,WK1=R0,WK2=R1  REQUESTS WE PROCESS:   M0019RLY
.LKCNT1B SPACE  2                                              M0043RLY
*
*        IF DESIRED, TRACE THIS LINK REQUEST.
*
         AIF    (NOT &SDIAG).LKTRC1A                           M0043RLY
         TM     MSTRCFLG,MSTRCLNK DO WE WANT LINK TRACING?     M0043RLY
         BZ     LKTRACE1          NO - SKIP PROCESSING HERE    M0043RLY
         CALL   LNKDSPTR          ALLOCATE TRACE TABLE ENTRY   M0043RLY
         BNZ    LKTRACE1          CC>0 ... NO TRACING NOW      M0043RLY
         USING  TRACE,R1          SET ADDRESSABILITY FOR THIS  M0043RLY
         MVI    TRFCODE,TRFLCALL  SET "LINK CALL" EVENT        M0043RLY
         LM     R2,R4,COMSVLNK    RELOAD CALLER'S R0-R2        M0019RLY
         STCM   R2,3,TRLCREG0     SAVE LOW BYTES OF R0         M0043RLY
         ST     R3,TRLCREG1       SAVE R1 VALUE PASSED         M0043RLY
         STC    R4,TRLCREG2       SAVE OPTIONS FROM R2         M0043RLY
         LM     R2,R5,LNKSVR12    RELOAD CALLER'S R12-R15      M0043RLY
         ST     R2,TRLCMODB       SAVE R12 AS CALLER'S BASE    M0043RLY
         ST     R4,TRLCFROM       SAVE R14 AS CALLER'S RETURN  M0043RLY
         ST     R5,TRLCTO         SAVE R15 AS CALLEE'S ADDRESS M0043RLY
         LTR    R13,R13           HAVE A CURRENT SAVEAREA?     M0043RLY
         BZ     *+12              NO - DON'T KNOW WHO WE ARE   M0043RLY
         L      R2,SAVECR15       GET PTR TO CALLER'S ENTRY    M0043RLY
         ST     R2,TRLCWHO        SAVE TO IDENTIFY THE CALLER  M0043RLY
         DROP   R1                (TRACE)                      M0043RLY
LKTRACE1 EQU    *                                              M0043RLY
.LKTRC1A ANOP  ,                                               M0043RLY
         SPACE  2
*
*        ALLOCATE A SAVE AREA AND LINK IT TO THE PREVIOUS ONE.
*
         LR     R3,R13            SAVE CURRENT SAVEAREA ADDRESS
         BAL    R9,GETSAVE        ALLOCATE A NEW SAVEAREA
         LTR    R3,R3             DO WE HAVE A PREVIOUS AREA?
         BZ     *+8               NO - LEAVE FORWARD PTR ALONE
         ST     R13,SAVEFW(,R3)   SET FORWARD POINTER IN PREVIOUS
         ST     R3,SAVEBW(,R13)   SET BACKWARD POINTER IN NEW AREA
         ST     R13,COMSVUSE      SAVE ADDRESS OF LATEST SAVEARM0019RLY
         SPACE  2
*
*        INVOKE THE CALLED ROUTINE.
*
         ST     R13,LNKSVR13      PASS SAVEAREA TO CALLEE IN R13
         MVC    SAVECR14,LNKSVR14 SAVE THE "TRUE" RETURN ADDRESS
         AIF   (&S$CMS OR &S$VMV).NOVMS12                       GP97338
         L     R1,SAVECR14   GET USER'S RETURN ADDRESS          GP97338
         SH    R1,=H'4'      BACK UP                            GP97338
         CLI   2(R1),X'07'   USER EXIT REQUEST CALL?            GP97338
         BE    LNKUEXIT      YES; HANDLE SLIGHTLY DIFFERENTLY   GP97338
.NOVMS12 ANOP  ,             IN VM HANDLE AS BEFORE             GP97338
         LA     R14,LNKLNKRT      POINT TO OUR RETURN ADDRESS
         ST     R14,LNKSVR14      SET FOR RETURN TO US
         LM     R0,R15,COMSVLNK   RELOAD CALLER'S REGISTERS    M0019RLY
         SPACE
         ST     R15,SAVECR15      SAVE ENTRY POINT ADDRESS     M0043RLY
         AIF    (&S$VTAM).LKDIAG1                              M0625RLY
         STCK   MSTCLOCK          SAVE CURRENT TOD CLOCK VALUE M0043RLY
         MVC    SAVETODC,MSTCLOCK+3    COPY SIGNIFICANT PART   M0043RLY
         AGO .LKDIAG2                                          M0625RLY
.LKDIAG1 ANOP
         STCK   LINTMCLK          SAVE CURRENT TOD CLOCK VALUE M0625RLY
         MVC    SAVETODC,LINTMCLK+3    COPY SIGNIFICANT PART   M0625RLY
.LKDIAG2 ANOP  ,                                               M0625RLY
         SPACE
         BR     R15               - INVOKE THE CALLED ROUTINE -
         SPACE 1     ,                                          GP97338
         AIF   (&S$CMS OR &S$VMV).NOVM12S                       GP97338
***********************************************************************
*                                                                     *
*  NOTES -                                                            *
*                                                                     *
*     THIS SECTION INVOKES AN EXTERNAL ROUTINE (E.G., A USER EXIT)    *
*     IN THE APPROPRIATE AMODE, AND PRESERVES OURS.                   *
*                                                                     *
*     INVOKE WITH   CALL (R5),EXIT   TO INVOKE TARGET IN ITS AMODE    *
*                                                                     *
***********************************************************************
LNKUEXIT STCK  LINTMCLK      GET CLOCK                          GP97338
         MVC   SAVETODC,LINTMCLK+3  SAVE A BIT                  GP97338
         LM    R0,R11,COMSVLNK  LOAD PARAMETER REGISTERS        GP97338
         LM    R13,R15,COMSVLNK+13*4  LOAD AMODE/ENTRY          GP97338
         SYNCH (R15),RESTORE=YES,AMODE=DEFINED  INVOKE USER EXIT  97338
         IPM   R5            GET PROGRAM MASK (USELESS)         GP97338
         ST    R15,COMSVLNK+15*4  SAVE RETURN CODE              GP97338
         STM   R0,R2,COMSVLNK  SAVE OTHER POSSIBLY ALTERED REGS gp97338
         B     LNKRT3        JOIN COMMON CODE                   GP97338
.NOVM12S ANOP  ,     ,                                          GP97338
         SPACE  2
*
*        FATAL ERROR: ATTEMPT TO CALL A NONEXISTANT ROUTINE.
*
LNK001   PABEND 001               *** INVALID CALL ATTEMPT ***
         EJECT
***********************************************************************
*                                                                     *
*                           L N K L N K R T                           *
*                                                                     *
*---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY POINT NAME -                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*        LNKLNKRT                                                     *
*                                                                     *
*  FUNCTION -                                                         *
*                                                                     *
*        PERFORM "RETURN" TYPE LINKAGE                                *
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY CONDITIONS -                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*        R8  = ADDRESS OF THE LINE BLOCK, IF PRESENT                  *
*        R10 = ADDRESS OF THE MASTER CONTROL BLOCK                    *
*                                                                     *
*  EXIT CONDITIONS -                                                  *
*                                                                     *
*        EXIT VIA RETURN TO CALLER ROUTINE (SEE NOTES BELOW).         *
*                                                                     *
*  REGISTER USAGE -                                                   *
*                                                                     *
*        R15   = ENTRY ADDRESS FOR LINKAGE & WORK                     *
*        R14   = RETURN ADDRESS FOR LINKAGE                           *
*        R13   = UNUSED                                               *
*        R12   = MODULE BASE ADDRESS                                  *
*        R11   = UNUSED                                               *
*        R10   = ADDRESS OF THE MASTER CONTROL BLOCK                  *
*        R9-R0 = WORK                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*  NOTES -                                                            *
*                                                                     *
*        1. THIS SUBROUTINE PROVIDES THE "RETURN" PROCESSING FOR      *
*           LINKAGE BETWEEN TWO ROUTINES (TERMED THE CALLER AND       *
*           SEE THE "LNKLNKLK" ROUTINE FOR MORE INFORMATION.          *
*                                                                     *
***********************************************************************
         SPACE  2
LNKLNKRT ENTER  BASE=,SAVE=            RETURN TO CALLING ROUTINE:
         SPACE  2
*
*        RETURN CONTROL FROM A CALLED ROUTINE: FIRST SETUP
*        CALLER'S REGISTERS IN A TEMPORARY SAVE AREA AND SAVE
*        THE CONDITION CODE. THEN RELOAD OUR MODULE'S BASE
*        REGISTER AND UPDATE VARIOUS LINKAGE STATISTICS.
*
         STM    R0,R15,COMSVLNK   PLACE REGISTERS IN TEMP AREA M0019RLY
         AIF (&S$TSO OR &S$VTAM).LNKR1                         F0812RLY
         L      R12,MSTLKBAS      LOAD MODULE BASE ADDRESS     ESA12RLY
         BM     CC1SAVE           GO SET CC=1 FLAG             ESA12RLY
         BP     CC2SAVE           GO SET CC=2 FLAG             ESA12RLY
         BO     CC3SAVE           GO SET CC=3 FLAG             ESA12RLY
         SPACE ,                                               ESA12RLY
CC0SAVE  EQU    *                 REMEMBER CC=0 WAS SET        ESA12RLY
         MVI    COMCC,COMCC0      SET CC VALUE                 ESA27RLY
         B      LNKRT1            AND CONTINUE                 ESA12RLY
         SPACE ,                                               ESA12RLY
CC1SAVE  EQU    *                 REMEMBER CC=1 WAS SET        ESA12RLY
         MVI    COMCC,COMCC1      SET CC VALUE                 ESA27RLY
         B      LNKRT1            AND CONTINUE                 ESA12RLY
         SPACE ,                                               ESA12RLY
CC2SAVE  EQU    *                 REMEMBER CC=2 WAS SET        ESA12RLY
         MVI    COMCC,COMCC2      SET CC VALUE                 ESA27RLY
         B      LNKRT1            AND CONTINUE                 ESA12RLY
         SPACE ,                                               ESA12RLY
CC3SAVE  EQU    *                 REMEMBER CC=3 WAS SET        ESA12RLY
         MVI    COMCC,COMCC3      SET CC VALUE                 ESA27RLY
         SPACE ,                                               ESA12RLY
LNKRT1   EQU    *                 CHECK FOR 370 OR XA...       ESA12RLY
         TM     X'5EA'(0),X'80'   TEST FOR XA VIRTUAL MACHINE  ESA12RLY
         BNO    LNKRT2            NO, GO SAVE 370 CC           ESA12RLY
         SPACE  ,                                              ESA12RLY
LNKRT10  EQU    *                 CHECK FOR CC=1               ESA12RLY
         CLI    COMCC,1           WAS IT CC=1?                 ESA27RLY
         BNE    LNKRT1A           NO, CHECK FOR CC=2           ESA12RLY
         CLI    *,FF              SET CC=1                     ESA12RLY
         B      LNKRT1D           AND GO SAVE IT...            ESA12RLY
         SPACE  ,                                              ESA12RLY
LNKRT1A  EQU    *                 CHECK FOR CC=2               ESA12RLY
         CLI    COMCC,2           WAS IT CC=2                  ESA27RLY
         BNE    LNKRT1B           NO, GO CHECK FOR CC=3        ESA12RLY
         CLI    *,0               SET CC=2                     ESA12RLY
         B      LNKRT1D           AND GO SAVE IT...            ESA12RLY
         SPACE  ,                                              ESA12RLY
LNKRT1B  EQU    *                 CHECK FOR CC=3               ESA12RLY
         CLI    COMCC,3           WAS IT CC=3                  ESA27RLY
         BNE    LNKRT1C           NO, GO SET IT TO CC=0        ESA12RLY
         TM     *+1,FF            SET CC=3                     ESA12RLY
         B      LNKRT1D           AND GO SAVE IT...            ESA12RLY
         SPACE  ,                                              ESA12RLY
LNKRT1C  EQU    *                 SET CC=0                     ESA12RLY
         SR     R5,R5             CLEAR AND SET TO 0           ESA12RLY
         SPACE  ,                                              ESA12RLY
LNKRT1D  EQU    *                 SAVE CC FOR XA MACHINE       ESA12RLY
         IPM    R5                SAVE XA CC                   ESA12RLY
         B      LNKRT3            AND CONTINUE                 ESA12RLY
         SPACE  ,                                              ESA12RLY
LNKRT2   EQU    *                 CHECK FOR CC=1               ESA12RLY
         CLI    COMCC,1           WAS IT CC=1?                 ESA27RLY
         BNE    LNKRT2A           NO, CHECK FOR CC=2           ESA12RLY
         CLI    *,FF              SET CC=1                     ESA12RLY
         B      LNKRT2D           AND GO SAVE IT...            ESA12RLY
         SPACE  ,                                              ESA12RLY
LNKRT2A  EQU    *                 CHECK FOR CC=2               ESA12RLY
         CLI    COMCC,2           WAS IT CC=2                  ESA27RLY
         BNE    LNKRT2B           NO, GO CHECK FOR CC=3        ESA12RLY
         CLI    *,0               SET CC=2                     ESA12RLY
         B      LNKRT2D           AND GO SAVE IT...            ESA12RLY
         SPACE  ,                                              ESA12RLY
LNKRT2B  EQU    *                 CHECK FOR CC=3               ESA12RLY
         CLI    COMCC,3           WAS IT CC=3                  ESA27RLY
         BNE    LNKRT2C           NO, GO SET IT TO CC=0        ESA12RLY
         TM     *+1,FF            SET CC=3                     ESA12RLY
         B      LNKRT2D           AND GO SAVE IT...            ESA12RLY
         SPACE  ,                                              ESA12RLY
LNKRT2C  EQU    *                 SET CC=0                     ESA12RLY
         SR     R5,R5             CLEAR AND SET TO 0           ESA12RLY
         SPACE  ,                                              ESA12RLY
LNKRT2D  EQU    *                 S/370 VIRTUAL MACHINE..      ESA12RLY
         BALR   R5,0              SAVE THE CONDITION CODE
         AGO .LNKR1A                                           F0812RLY
.LNKR1   ANOP  ,                                               F0812RLY
         IPM    R5                Save the condition code      M0825RLY
         L      R12,MSTLKBAS      LOAD MODULE BASE ADDRESS     F0812RLY
.LNKR1A  ANOP  ,                                               F0812RLY
         SPACE  ,                                              ESA12RLY
LNKRT3   EQU     *                CHECK FOR PROPER LINKAGE     ESA12RLY
         LTR    R13,R13           CHECK THE SAVEAREA ADDRESS
         BZ     LNK002            ZERO - LINKAGE ERROR         M0339RLY
         ICM    R2,15,LNKSVR12    CHECK CALLER'S R12           M0339RLY
         BZ     LNK002            ZERO - LINKAGE ERROR
         SPACE  2                                              M0019RLY
         AIF    (NOT &SDIAG).RTCNT1B                           M0019RLY
*
*        SAVE DIAGNOSTIC INFORMATION
*
RTCOUNTS CSADD  MSTLKNMR,WK1=R0,WK2=R1  REQUESTS WE PROCESS:   M0019RLY
.RTCNT1B SPACE  2                                              M0043RLY
*
*        IF DESIRED, TRACE THIS LINK REQUEST.
*
         AIF    (NOT &SDIAG).RTTRC1A                           M0043RLY
         TM     MSTRCFLG,MSTRCLNK DO WE WANT LINK TRACING?     M0043RLY
         BZ     RTTRACE1          NO - SKIP PROCESSING HERE    M0043RLY
         CALL   LNKDSPTR          ALLOCATE TRACE TABLE ENTRY   M0043RLY
         BNZ    RTTRACE1          CC>0 ... NO TRACING NOW      M0043RLY
         USING  TRACE,R1          SET ADDRESSABILITY FOR THIS  M0043RLY
         MVI    TRFCODE,TRFLRETN  SET "LINK RETURN" EVENT      M0043RLY
         LM     R2,R3,COMSVLNK    RELOAD RETURNED R0-R1        M0019RLY
         STCM   R2,3,TRLRREG0     SAVE LOW BYTES OF R0         M0043RLY
         ST     R3,TRLRREG1       SAVE R1 VALUE RETURNED       M0043RLY
         L      R2,LNKSVR12       RELOAD CALLER'S R12          M0043RLY
         ST     R2,TRLRMODB       SAVE AS CALLER'S BASE        M0043RLY
         L      R2,SAVECR14       GET "TRUE" RETURN ADDRESS    M0043RLY
         ST     R2,TRLRTO         SAVE AS CALLER'S RETURN      M0043RLY
         L      R2,LNKSVR15       GET RETURNED R15 VALUE       M0043RLY
         STC    R2,TRLRCODE       SAVE AS RETURN CODE          M0043RLY
         L      R2,SAVECR15       GET SAVED ENTRY ADDRESS      M0043RLY
         ST     R2,TRLRFROM       SAVE TO IDENTIFY CALLEE      M0043RLY
         ICM    R3,15,SAVEBKWD    ADDRESS PREVIOUS SAVEAREA    M0043RLY
         BZ     *+12              ZERO - CAN'T IDENTIFY CALLER M0043RLY
         L      R2,SAVECR15-SAVEAREA(,R3) GET PTR TO CALLER    M0043RLY
         ST     R2,TRLRWHO        SAVE TO IDENTIFY THE CALLER  M0043RLY
         DROP   R1                (TRACE)                      M0043RLY
RTTRACE1 EQU    *                                              M0043RLY
.RTTRC1A ANOP  ,                                               M0043RLY
         SPACE  2
*
*        FREE THE SAVE AREA.
*
         L      R0,SAVECR14       RESTORE "TRUE" RETURN ADDRESS
         ST     R0,LNKSVR14       PASS BACK TO CALLER IN R14
         BAL    R9,FREESAVE       GO TO FREE UP THE SAVE AREA
         ST     R13,COMSVUSE      SET PREVIOUS AS NEW AREA     M0019RLY
         ST     R13,LNKSVR13      PASS BACK TO CALLER IN R13
         SPACE  2
*
*        RETURN TO THE CALLING ROUTINE.
*
         SPM    R5                RESTORE THE SAVED CONDITION CODE
         LM     R0,R15,COMSVLNK   RESTORE SAVED REGISTERS      M0019RLY
         BR     R14               - RETURN TO CALLING ROUTINE -
         SPACE  2
*
*        FATAL ERROR: INVALID RETURN LINKAGE USED.
*
LNK002   PABEND 002               *** INVALID RETURN LINKAGE ***
         EJECT
***********************************************************************
*                                                                     *
*                           L N K L N K S A                           *
*                                                                     *
*---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY POINT NAME -                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*        LNKLNKSA                                                     *
*                                                                     *
*  FUNCTION -                                                         *
*                                                                     *
*        ALLOCATE A NEW SAVE AREA                                     *
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY CONDITIONS -                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*        R13 = ADDRESS OF THE OLD SAVEAREA                            *
*        R14 = CALLER'S RETURN ADDRESS                                *
*        R15 = ENTRY POINT ADDRESS, =A(LNKLNKSA)                      *
*                                                                     *
*  EXIT CONDITIONS -                                                  *
*                                                                     *
*        R13 = ADDRESS OF THE NEW SAVEAREA                            *
*        R15 = 0; THIS IS ALWAYS SUCCESSFUL                           *
*                                                                     *
*  REGISTER USAGE -                                                   *
*                                                                     *
*        R15   = ENTRY ADDRESS FOR LINKAGE & WORK                     *
*        R14   = RETURN ADDRESS FOR LINKAGE                           *
*        R13   = SAVE AREA ADDRESS                                    *
*        R12   = MODULE BASE ADDRESS                                  *
*        R11   = UNUSED                                               *
*        R10   = ADDRESS OF THE MASTER CONTROL BLOCK                  *
*        R9-R0 = WORK                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*  NOTES -                                                            *
*                                                                     *
*        1. THIS SUBROUTINE ALLOCATES A NEW SAVEAREA AND RETURNS      *
*           IT TO OUR CALLER. THE PREVIOUS SAVE AREA IS LINKED TO     *
*           THE NEW SAVE AREA FOR LATER RESTORATION.                  *
*                                                                     *
***********************************************************************
         SPACE  2
LNKLNKSA ENTER  SAVE=COMSVLNK     ALLOCATE A SAVE AREA:        M0019RLY
         SPACE  2
*
*        ALLOCATE A SAVE AREA AND LINK IT TO THE PREVIOUS ONE.
*
         LR     R3,R13            SAVE CURRENT SAVEAREA ADDRESS
         BAL    R9,GETSAVE        ALLOCATE A NEW SAVEAREA
         LTR    R3,R3             DO WE HAVE A PREVIOUS AREA?
         BZ     *+8               NO - LEAVE FORWARD PTR ALONE
         ST     R13,SAVEFW(,R3)   SET FORWARD POINTER IN PREVIOUS
         ST     R3,SAVEBW(,R13)   SET BACKWARD POINTER IN NEW AREA
         ST     R13,COMSVUSE      STORE SAVEAREA ADDR IN USE   M0388RLY
         SPACE  ,                                              M0043RLY
         AIF    (NOT &SDIAG).SADIAG1                           M0043RLY
         LTR    R15,R3            DO WE HAVE A PREVIOUS AREA?  M0019RLY
         BZ     *+8               NO - NO KNOWN ENTRY POINT    M0019RLY
         L      R15,SAVECR15-SAVEAREA(,R3)  GET ENTRY ADDRESS  M0019RLY
         ST     R15,SAVECR15      SAVE LAST KNOWN ENTRY ADDR.  M0019RLY
.SADIAG1 ANOP   ,                                              M0043RLY
         SPACE  2
*
*        RETURN THE NEW SAVEAREA TO OUR CALLER.
*
         ST     R13,LNKSVR13           PASS BACK THE AREA ADDRESS
         RETURN RC=0,SAVE=COMSVLNK     - RETURN TO OUR CALLER -M0019RLY
         EJECT
***********************************************************************
*                                                                     *
*                           L N K L N K S R                           *
*                                                                     *
*---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY POINT NAME -                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*        LNKLNKSR                                                     *
*                                                                     *
*  FUNCTION -                                                         *
*                                                                     *
*        RETURN THE CURRENT SAVE AREA                                 *
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY CONDITIONS -                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*        R13 = ADDRESS OF THE CURRENT SAVEAREA                        *
*        R14 = CALLER'S RETURN ADDRESS                                *
*        R15 = ENTRY POINT ADDRESS, =A(LNKLNKSR)                      *
*                                                                     *
*  EXIT CONDITIONS -                                                  *
*                                                                     *
*        R13 = ADDRESS OF THE OLD SAVEAREA                            *
*        R15 = 0; THIS IS ALWAYS SUCCESSFUL                           *
*                                                                     *
*  REGISTER USAGE -                                                   *
*                                                                     *
*        R15   = ENTRY ADDRESS FOR LINKAGE & WORK                     *
*        R14   = RETURN ADDRESS FOR LINKAGE                           *
*        R13   = SAVE AREA ADDRESS                                    *
*        R12   = MODULE BASE ADDRESS                                  *
*        R11   = UNUSED                                               *
*        R10   = ADDRESS OF THE MASTER CONTROL BLOCK                  *
*        R9-R0 = WORK                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*  NOTES -                                                            *
*                                                                     *
*        1. THIS SUBROUTINE RETURNS THE CURRENT SAVEAREA TO THE       *
*           POOL OF AVAILABLE AREAS. THE PREVIOUS SAVE AREA IS        *
*           RETURNED TO OUR CALLER.                                   *
*                                                                     *
***********************************************************************
         SPACE  2
LNKLNKSR ENTER  SAVE=COMSVLNK     RETURN A SAVE AREA:          M0019RLY
         SPACE  2
*
*        UNCHAIN THE PREVIOUS SAVE AREA AND RETURN THE CURRENT ONE.
*
         BAL    R9,FREESAVE       FREE THE CURRENT SAVEAREA
         ST     R13,LNKSVR13      PASS BACK THE PREVIOUS AREA
         ST     R13,COMSVUSE      STORE SAVEAREA ADDR IN USE   M0388RLY
         SPACE  2
*
*        RETURN THE OLD SAVEAREA TO OUR CALLER.
*
         RETURN RC=0,SAVE=COMSVLNK     - RETURN TO OUR CALLER -M0019RLY
         EJECT
***********************************************************************
*                                                                     *
*                           L N K L N K T R                           *
*                                                                     *
*---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY POINT NAME -                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*        LNKLNKTR                                                     *
*                                                                     *
*  FUNCTION -                                                         *
*                                                                     *
*        TERMINATE THE LINKAGE MANAGER                                *
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY CONDITIONS -                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*        R14 = CALLER'S RETURN ADDRESS                                *
*        R15 = ENTRY POINT ADDRESS, =A(LNKLNKTR)                      *
*                                                                     *
*  EXIT CONDITIONS -                                                  *
*                                                                     *
*        R15 = 0; THIS IS ALWAYS SUCCESSFUL (CC=0).                   *
*                                                                     *
*  REGISTER USAGE -                                                   *
*                                                                     *
*        R15   = ENTRY ADDRESS FOR LINKAGE & WORK                     *
*        R14   = RETURN ADDRESS FOR LINKAGE                           *
*        R13   = UNUSED                                               *
*        R12   = MODULE BASE ADDRESS                                  *
*        R11   = UNUSED                                               *
*        R10   = ADDRESS OF THE MASTER CONTROL BLOCK                  *
*        R9-R8 = UNUSED                                               *
*        R7-R0 = WORK                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*  NOTES -                                                            *
*                                                                     *
*        NONE.                                                        *
*                                                                     *
***********************************************************************
         SPACE  2
LNKLNKTR ENTER  SAVE=COMSVLNK     TERMINATE LINKAGE MANAGEMENT:M0019RLY
         SPACE  2                                              M0019RLY
         AIF (&S$VTAM).TRFREE1                                 M0019RLY
*
*        FREE THE BLOCK OF PREALLOCATED SAVE AREAS.
*
         LM     R0,R1,MSTSVARS    LOAD SIZE & ADDRESS OF AREA
         CALL   LNKSTGFR          FREE UP THE ALLOCATED AREA
.TRFREE1 ANOP   ,                                              M0019RLY
         SPACE  2
*
*        LINKAGE TERMINATION IS NOW COMPLETE.
*
         RETURN RC=0,SAVE=COMSVLNK     - RETURN TO OUR CALLER -M0019RLY
         EJECT
***********************************************************************
*                                                                     *
*                           L N K L N K X C                           *
*                                                                     *
*---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY POINT NAME -                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*        LNKLNKXC                                                     *
*                                                                     *
*  FUNCTION -                                                         *
*                                                                     *
*        PERFORM "XCTL" TYPE LINKAGE                                  *
*                                                                     *
*  ENTRY CONDITIONS -                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*        R14 = CALLER'S RETURN ADDRESS (SEE NOTES BELOW).             *
*        R15 = ENTRY POINT ADDRESS, =A(LNKLNKXC)                      *
*                                                                     *
*  EXIT CONDITIONS -                                                  *
*                                                                     *
*        EXIT VIA BRANCH TO CALLEE ROUTINE (SEE NOTES BELOW).         *
*                                                                     *
*  REGISTER USAGE -                                                   *
*                                                                     *
*        R15   = ENTRY ADDRESS FOR LINKAGE & WORK                     *
*        R14   = RETURN ADDRESS FOR LINKAGE                           *
*        R13   = UNUSED                                               *
*        R12   = MODULE BASE ADDRESS                                  *
*        R11   = UNUSED                                               *
*        R10   = ADDRESS OF THE MASTER CONTROL BLOCK                  *
*        R9-R0 = WORK                                                 *
*                                                                     *
*  NOTES -                                                            *
*                                                                     *
*        1. THIS SUBROUTINE PROVIDES BRANCH-WITHOUT-RETURN LINKAGE    *
*           BETWEEN TWO ROUTINES (TERMED THE CALLER AND THE CALLEE).  *
*           THE CALLEE IS PASSED REGISTER VALUES OBTAINED FROM THE    *
*           CALLER'S SAVE AREA (THE CALLER'S CALLER, THAT IS).        *
*                                                                     *
*        2. THE CALLEE'S ADDRESS IS DETERMINED BY EXECUTING THE       *
*           INSTRUCTION JUST AFTER THE "BAL" TO THIS ROUTINE.         *
*           THAT IS, THE INSTRUCTION AT 0(R14) ON ENTRY HERE. NO      *
*           RETURN WILL BE MADE; THE "RETURN ADDRESS" IN R14 IS       *
*           USED SOLELY TO LOCATE THE CALLEE.                         *
*                                                                     *
*        3. ALSO REFER TO THE "LNKLNKLK" ROUTINE FOR ADDITIONAL       *
*           INFORMATION.                                              *
*                                                                     *
***********************************************************************
         SPACE  2
LNKLNKXC ENTER  BASE=,SAVE=       TRANSFER CONTROL ONWARD:
         SPACE  2
*
*        CALL A PEER-ROUTINE: FIRST LOAD THE CALLEE'S ADDRESS,
*        UPDATE OUR CALLER'S RETURN ADDRESS, AND SAVE THE
*        CALLER'S REGISTERS (TEMPORARILY). THEN RELOAD OUR
*        MODULE'S BASE REGISTER AND UPDATE VARIOUS LINKAGE
*        STATISTICS.
*
         EX     0,0(R14)          EXECUTE TO LOCATE CALLEE
         LA     R14,4(,R14)       AND INCREMENT RETURN ADDRESS
         LA     R15,0(,R15)       PURIFY CALLEE'S ADDRESS VALUE
         A      R15,MSTRELOC      RELOCATE THE ADDRESS CONSTANT
         L      R12,MSTLKBAS      LOAD MODULE BASE ADDRESS
         CL     R15,MSTRELOC      HAD ZERO FOR CALLEE'S ADDRESS?
         BZ     LNK003            YES - CALLEE DOES NOT EXIST
         SPACE  2                                              M0019RLY
         AIF    (NOT &SDIAG).XFCNT1B                           M0019RLY
*
*        SAVE DIAGNOSTIC INFORMATION
*
XFCOUNTS CSADD  MSTLKNMX,WK1=R0,WK2=R1  REQUESTS WE PROCESS:   M0019RLY
.XFCNT1B SPACE  2
*
*        INVOKE THE CALLED ROUTINE.
*
         L      R14,SAVER14       LOAD REGISTERS FROM SAVE AREA
         LM     R0,R12,SAVER0     ...
         BR     R15               - INVOKE THE CALLED ROUTINE -
         SPACE  2
*
*        FATAL ERROR: ATTEMPT TO XCTL A NONEXISTANT ROUTINE.
*
LNK003   PABEND 003               *** INVALID XCTL ATTEMPT ***
         EJECT
***********************************************************************
*                                                                     *
*                 LOCAL SUBROUTINE TO FREE A SAVE AREA                *
*                                                                     *
***********************************************************************
*
*  SUBROUTINE NAME -
*
*        FREESAVE
*
*  FUNCTION -
*
*        FREE A SAVE AREA
*
*  ENTRY CONDITIONS -
*
*        R9  = CALLER'S RETURN ADDRESS
*        R13 = ADDRESS OF THE CURRENT SAVE AREA
*
*  EXIT CONDITIONS -
*
*        R13 = ADDRESS OF THE PREVIOUS SAVE AREA
*
*  REGISTERS DESTROYED -
*
*        R0  R1  R2
*
*  NOTES -
*
*        1. THIS SUBROUTINE WILL FREE A SAVE AREA PREVIOUSLY
*           ALLOCATED BY THE "GETSAVE" ROUTINE. REFER TO THAT
*           ROUTINE FOR ADDITIONAL INFORMATION.
*
FREESAVE DS     0H                RETURN A SAVE AREA:
*
*        FREE THE SAVE AREA. PREALLOCATED AREAS ARE RETURN TO
*        THE AVAILABLE SAVEAREA CHAIN. OTHER AREAS ARE RETURNED
*        TO FREE STORAGE.
*
         L      R2,SAVEBKWD       LOAD PREVIOUS AREA ADDRESS
         TM     SAVEFLAG,SAVEFREE AREA ALLOCATED FROM FREE STORAGE?
         BNZ    FRESAVE1          YES - GO TO FREE IT UP
         MVC    SAVELINK,COMSVFRE SET AT FRONT OF "FREE" CHAIN M0019RLY
         ST     R13,COMSVFRE      ...                          M0019RLY
         B      FRESAVE2          - THAT'S ALL FOR NOW -
         SPACE
FRESAVE1 EQU    *                 RETURN SAVEAREA TO FREE STORAGE:
         LA     R0,SAVESIZE       LOAD SIZE OF THE SAVEAREA
         LR     R1,R13            COPY AREA ADDRESS
         CALL   LNKSTGFR          GO TO FREE ALLOCATED STORAGE
         SPACE
FRESAVE2 EQU    *                 THE SAVEAREA HAS BEEN FREED:
         LR     R13,R2            RETURN THE PREVIOUS SAVEAREA
         BR     R9                - RETURN TO OUR CALLER -
         EJECT
***********************************************************************
*                                                                     *
*              LOCAL SUBROUTINE TO ALLOCATE A SAVE AREA               *
*                                                                     *
***********************************************************************
*
*  SUBROUTINE NAME -
*
*        GETSAVE
*
*  FUNCTION -
*
*        ALLOCATE A SAVE AREA
*
*  ENTRY CONDITIONS -
*
*        R9 = CALLER'S RETURN ADDRESS
*
*  EXIT CONDITIONS -
*
*        R13 = ADDRESS OF THE NEW SAVE AREA
*
*  REGISTERS DESTROYED -
*
*        R0  R1  R2
*
*  NOTES -
*
*        1. THIS SUBROUTINE WILL ALLOCATE A SAVE AREA FOR USE
*           BY OUR CALLER. WE PREFER A PREALLOCATED SAVE AREA
*           BUT WILL ALLOCATE ONE FROM FREE STORAGE IF NEEDED.
*
GETSAVE  DS     0H                ALLOCATE A SAVE AREA:
         ICM    R13,15,COMSVFRE   LOAD FIRST FREE AREA ADDRESS M0019RLY
         BZ     GETSAVE1          ZERO - NEED TO ALLOCATE ONE
         L      R1,SAVELINK       GET NEXT FREE AREA ADDRESS
         ST     R1,COMSVFRE       THIS IS NOW THE FIRST FREE   M0019RLY
         SR     R2,R2             CLEAR VALUE FOR "SAVEFLAG"
         B      GETSAVE2          - GO USE FREE AREA -
         SPACE
GETSAVE1 EQU    *                 ALLOCATE A NEW SAVE AREA:
         LA     R0,SAVESIZE       LOAD SIZE NEEDED FOR THIS
         LA     R2,ALCZERO+ALABERR AND OPTIONS FOR ALLOCATION
         CALL   LNKSTGAL          GO ALLOCATE STORAGE AREA
         LR     R13,R1            COPY THE AREA ADDRESS
         LA     R2,SAVEFREE       GET VALUE FOR "SAVEFLAG"
         SPACE
GETSAVE2 EQU    *                 WE NOW HAVE A SAVE AREA:
         STC    R2,SAVEFLAG       SET SAVEAREA FLAGS
         BR     R9                - RETURN TO OUR CALLER -
         EJECT
***********************************************************************
*                                                                     *
*                         COMMON MODULE DATA                          *
*                                                                     *
***********************************************************************
         SPACE  2                                              M0019RLY
         AIF (&S$CMS OR &S$TSO).DATA1                          M0019RLY
*
*        PARM LIST FOR TASK ATTACHMENT.
*
ATTCHLST ATTACH EPLOC=0,ETXR=0,SF=L                            M0019RLY
ATTCHEND EQU    *                                              M0019RLY
.DATA1   ANOP   ,                                              M0019RLY
         SPACE  2
         LTORG  ,                 GENERATE LITERAL POOL:
         EJECT
***********************************************************************
*                                                                     *
*                         COMMON DEFINITIONS                          *
*                                                                     *
***********************************************************************
         SPACE  2
         COPY   EQUATES           COMMON EQUATE DEFINITIONS:
         COPY   LINE              LINE CONTROL BLOCK DEFINITION:
         COPY   MASTER            MASTER CONTROL BLOCK DEFINITION:
         COPY   SAVEAREA          SAVE AREA DEFINITION:
         COPY   TRACE             TRACE TABLE ENTRY DEFINITION:M0043RLY
         SPACE  2
*
*        EQUATES SPECIFIC TO THE LNKLNK MODULE
*
PRESAVE  EQU    16                NUMBER OF PREALLOCATED SAVE AREAS
         SPACE  2
*
*        REDEFINITIONS FOR THE LNKLNK MODULE
*
LNKSVR2  EQU    COMSVLNK+2*4      SAVE FOR REGISTER 2          M0019RLY
LNKSVR12 EQU    COMSVLNK+12*4     SAVE FOR REGISTER 12         M0019RLY
LNKSVR13 EQU    COMSVLNK+13*4     SAVE FOR REGISTER 13         M0019RLY
LNKSVR14 EQU    COMSVLNK+14*4     SAVE FOR REGISTER 14         M0019RLY
LNKSVR15 EQU    COMSVLNK+15*4     SAVE FOR REGISTER 15         M0019RLY
         SPACE  3
*                                                              ESA27RLY
*        THE FOLLOWING FIELDS LIE IN THE MASTER BLOCK FOR THE  ESA27RLY
*        'NATIVE' PRODUCTS AND IN THE LINE BLOCK FOR THE VTAM  ESA27RLY
*        VERSIONS.                                             ESA27RLY
*                                                              ESA27RLY
         AIF    (&S$VTAM).REDEF1                               ESA27RLY
COMCC    EQU    MSTCC          REDEFINE CC FIELD               ESA27RLY
COMCC0   EQU    MSTCC0         REDEFINE CC=0 VALUE             ESA27RLY

         AGO    .REDEF2                                        ESA27RLY
.REDEF1  ANOP   ,                                              ESA27RLY
