         SPACE 1                                                GP98108
         MACRO ,                                                GP98108
&NM      TUTX  &N,&VAL,&TEXT,&NP=1                              GP98108
         LCLC  &L                                               GP98108
&L       SETC  'L'''                                            GP98108
         AIF   ('&NM' EQ '').NOLAB                              GP98108
&NM      DS    0X                                               GP98108
.NOLAB   ANOP  ,                                                GP98108
TUALLO&N DC    YL2(&VAL,&NP)                                    GP98108
         AIF   ('&TEXT' EQ '').NOTEXT                           GP98108
         DC    YL2(&L.TUTX&N)                                   GP98108
TUTX&N   DC    &TEXT                                            GP98108
.NOTEXT  ANOP  ,                                                GP98108

         MEND  ,                                                GP98108
         EJECT
         COPY GLOBALS
         EJECT

*        ENTRY POINT NAME:
*
*              LNKS99DY
*
*        FUNCTION:
*
*              DYNAMIC ALLOCATION ROUTINE   (SVC 99)
*
*
*        REGISTER USAGE:
*
*               ENTRY:
*                          R1   -  PARAMETER LIST ADDRESS
*                          R8   -  LINE CONTROL BLOCK
*                          R10  -  MASTER CONTROL BLOCK
*                          R13  -  SAVE AREA ADDRESS
*                          R14  -  RETURN ADDRESS
*                          R15  -  ENTRY POINT ADDRESS
*
*               INTERNAL:
*                          R3   -  REQUEST BLOCK PTR ADDRESS
*                          R4   -  REQUEST BLOCK ADDRESS
*                          R5   -  TEXT UNIT PTR ADDRESS
*                          R6   -  TEXT UNIT ADDRESS
*                          R7   -  PARAMETER LIST ADDRESS
*                          R9   -  SUBROUTINE RETURN ADDRESS
*                          R12  -  BASE ADDRESS
*                          R13  -  NEW SAVE AREA ADDRESS
*                          R14  -  WORK REGISTER
*                          R15  -  WORK REGISTER
*
*               EXIT:
*                          R15  -  RETURN CODE
*                                  0  =  ALL OK (CC=0),
*                                  8  =  FILE ALLOC ERROR (CC=8)
*
**********************************************************************
         SPACE 2
LNKS99DY ENTER                   BEGIN THE PROGRAM:
         SPACE 2
         LR    R7,R1                   SET PARAMETER LIST BASE ADDRESS
         L     R3,R99WADDR             POINT TO A WORK AREA
         SPACE 2
*******************************************************************
*             (4   - BYTE REQUEST BLOCK POINTER AREA)
*             (20  - BYTE REQUEST BLOCK AREA)
*             (120 - BYTE TEXT UNIT POINTER AREA - 30 PTRS)
*             (240 - BYTE TEXT UNIT AREA)
*******************************************************************
         LA    R4,S99RBPTR+4           LOAD REQUEST BLOCK ADDRESS
         ST    R4,S99RBPTR             SAVE REQUEST BLOCK ADDRESS
         OI    S99RBPTR,S99RBPND       TAINT HIGH ORDER BIT
         XC    S99RB(S99RBLEN),S99RB   INITIALIZE REQUEST BLOCK AREA
         MVI   S99RBLN,S99RBLEN        SET PARM AREA LENGTH
         LA    R5,S99RB+S99RBLEN       POINT TO TEXT UNIT PTR LIST
         ST    R5,S99TXTPP             STORE TU PTR LIST ADDR IN RB
         LA    R6,S99RBPTR+144         LOAD ADDRESS FIRST TEXT UNIT
         ST    R6,S99TUPTR             SAVE ADDRESS IN TU PTR LIST
         TM    R99PRCSS,R99ALLOC       ALLOCATION REQUESTED
         BC    8,UNALLRTN              NO, GO CHECK FOR UNALLOCATION
         SPACE 2
*******************************************************************
*             DATASET ALLOCATION SECTION BEGINS HERE
*******************************************************************
         MVI   S99VERB,S99VRBAL        SET FOR DYNAMIC ALLOCATION
         TM    R99AFLG1,R99MOUNT       DO WE HAVE MOUNT AUTHORITY?
         BNZ   *+8                     YES - BRANCH
         OI    S99FLAG1,S99NOMNT       SUPPRESS MOUNTS
         SPACE 2
*******************************************************************
*      DDNAME TEXT UNIT BUILD AREA
*******************************************************************
         MVC   0(TUALNG01,R6),TUALLO01 SET DDNAME TU FIXED PORTION
         LA    R6,TUALNG01(R6)         POINT TO LENGTH TU LNG FIELD
         LA    R15,R99DDNAM            LOAD ADDRESS OF DDNAME
         LA    R14,8                   LOAD FULL FIELD LENGTH
         BAL   R9,FINDLNG              GO FIND FIELD LENGTH
         SPACE
         TM    R99AFLG1,R99INRDR       INTERNAL RDR REQUESTED? M0770RLY
         BC    1,*+12                  YES, BRANCH AROUND THIS M0770RLY
         TM    R99AFLG1,R99SYSOT       SYSOUT DATASET?
         BC    8,BUILDDSN              NO, GO BUILD DSN TU
         SPACE 2

         LA    R5,S99TUPL+4            GET ADDRESS OF NEXT TU PTR
         ST    R6,S99TUPTR             SAVE NXT ADDR IN TU PTR LIST
         MVC   0(TUALNG18,R6),TUALLO18 REQUEST SYSOUT DATASET
         TM    R99CLASS,255-C' ' CLASS SUPPLIED?                GP98108

         SPACE 2

         SPACE 2

BUILDDSN DS   0H
         SPACE 2                                                GP97226
***********************************************************************
*                                                                     *
*   THIS CODE INSERTION FIXES A PROBLEM WITH GDG HANDLING.            *
*                                                                     *
*   BY IBM DESIGN, THE CURRENT GDG LEVEL (0) REMAINS LINKED TO THE    *
*   TRUE NAME (GNNNNVNN) AT THE FIRST REQUEST FOR THE DURATION OF     *
*   THE JOB OR SESSION.  WITH THE OLD CODE, A (0) DOWNLOAD WOULD      *
*   ALWAYS GET THE SAME DATASET EVEN IF NEW GENERATIONS HAD BEEN      *
*   ADDED DURING THE SESSION.                                         *
*                                                                     *
*   THE FIX USES THE CATALOG LOCATE SERVICE TO GET THE TRUE NAME FOR  *
*   THE REQUESTED GENERATION AND USES THAT FOR THE ALLOCATION.        *
*                                                                     *
*   IBM HAS ANNOUNCED THAT SVC 26 IS NO LONGER SUPPORTED, AND MAY BE  *
*   DISCONTINUED IN A FUTURE RELEASE (USED BY LOCATE MACRO)           *
*                                                                     *
***********************************************************************
         TM    R99GDGN,255-BLNK  GENERATION NUMBER SUPPLIED?    GP97226
         BZ    DONEGDG       NO; SKIP ALL THIS                  GP97226
 OI S99FLG11,S99GDGNT  USE CURRENT BASE FOR GENERATION LOOK-UP  GP00141
         LA    R9,CAMEND-CAMSECT  GET SIZE OF WORK AREA         GP97226
         GETMAIN R,LV=(R9),LOC=BELOW   GET WORK SPACE           GP97253
         LR    R2,R1         PRESERVE THE STORAGE ADDRESS       GP97226
         USING CAMSECT,R2    DECLARE THE WORK AREA              GP97226
         LM    R14,R1,CAMPAT  GET PATTERN CAMLST                GP97226
         LA    R1,CAMWORK    POINT TO WORK AREA                 GP97226
         LA    R15,CAMDSN    POINT TO JCL FORMAT DSN            GP97226
         STM   R14,R1,CAMLST  BUILD COMPLETE REQUEST LIST       GP97226
         MVC   CAMDSN,R99DSN  MOVE NAME TO BE MOGRIFIED         GP97226
         LA    R14,L'CAMDSN  SET LENGTH OF DSN                  GP97226
         AR    R15,R14       POINT TO LAST BYTE +               GP97226
LOOPGDG  BCTR  R15,0         BACK UP                            GP97226
         CLI   0(R15),BLNK   TRAILING BLANK?                    GP97226
         BNE   LOPGDG        YES; FOUND INSERTION POINT         GP97226
         BCT   R14,LOOPGDG   TRY AGAIN                          GP97226
         B     MAINGDG       ALL BLANK ?                        GP97226
LOPGDG   CH    R14,=H'35'    ENOUGH ROOM FOR GENERATION NUMBER? GP97226
         BH    MAINGDG       NO; LET IT BE                      GP97226
         MVI   1(R15),C'('   START OF NUMBER                    GP97226
         CLI   R99GDGN,C'0'  IS THERE A DIGIT?                  GP97226
         BL    NUMGDG        NO; PROBABLY PLUS?                 GP97226
         MVI   2(R15),C'-'   RESTORE RELATIVITY                 GP97226
         LA    R15,1(,R15)   SKIP OVER IT                       GP97226
NUMGDG   MVC   2(L'R99GDGN,R15),R99GDGN  MOVE NUMBER            GP97226
         LA    R15,CAMDSN+L'CAMDSN  POINT PAST DSN              GP97226
         LA    R14,L'CAMDSN  SET LENGTH OF DSN                  GP97226
LOOPGEN  BCTR  R15,0         BACK UP                            GP97226
         CLI   0(R15),BLNK   TRAILING BLANK?                    GP97226
         BNE   LOPGEN        YES; FOUND INSERTION POINT         GP97226
         BCT   R14,LOOPGEN   TRY AGAIN                          GP97226
         B     MAINGDG       ALL BLANK ?                        GP97226
LOPGEN   MVI   1(R15),C')'   COMPLETE NAME                      GP97226
***>>> LOCATE REPLACED - DONE BY S99GDGNT FLAG                  GP00141
*        AMODESW MODE=24     MAKE SURE                          GP97253
*OLD*    LOCATE CAMLST       DO THE LOCATE                      GP97226
*        AMODESW MODE=31,REG=R14   RESTORE                      GP97253
*OLD*    BXH   R15,R15,MAINGDG  FAILED - PROCEED AS BEFORE      GP97226
         MVC   R99DSN,CAMDSN  UPDATE WITH RETURNED TRUE NAME    GP97226
         XC    R99GDGN,R99GDGN                                  GP97226
         B     MAINGDG       SKIP AROUND CAMLST PATTERN         GP97226
         SPACE 1                                                GP97226
CAMPAT   CAMLST NAME,R99DSN-R99DSN,,CAMWORK-CAMWORK  PATTERN    GP97226
MAINGDG  FREEMAIN R,A=(R2),LV=(R9)  FREE WORK AREA              GP97226
DONEGDG  DS    0H                                               GP97226

*      UNIT TEXT UNIT BUILD AREA
*******************************************************************
CHK4UNIT EQU   *
         TM    R99UNIT,255-C' '  UNIT SPECIFIED?                GP98108
         BZ    CHKFVOLS          NO, GO CHECK FOR VOLSERS       GP98108
         LA    R5,S99TUPL+4            GET ADDRESS OF NEXT TU PTR
         ST    R6,S99TUPTR             SAVE NXT ADDR IN TU PTR LIST
         MVC   0(TUALNG15,R6),TUALLO15 SET UNIT TU FIXED PORTION
         LA    R6,TUALNG15(R6)         POINT TO LENGTH TU LNG FIELD
         LA    15,R99UNIT              LOAD ADDRESS OF UNIT
         LA    R14,8                   LOAD FULL FIELD LENGTH
         BAL   R9,FINDLNG              GO FIND FIELD LENGTH
         SPACE 2
*******************************************************************

         LA    R5,S99TUPL+4            GET ADDRESS OF NEXT TU PTR
         ST    R6,S99TUPTR             SAVE NXT ADDR IN TU PTR LIST
         MVC   0(TUALNG10,R6),TUALLO10 SET VOLSER TU FIXED PORTION
         ST    R6,R99TUPSV             SAVE TEXT UNIT POSITION
         LA    R6,TUALNG10(R6)         POINT TO LENGTH TU LNG FIELD
         LA    15,R99VOLS1             LOAD ADDRESS OF VOLSER #1
         LA    R14,6                   LOAD FULL FIELD LENGTH
         BAL   R9,FINDLNG              GO FIND FIELD LENGTH
         SPACE 2

ALLCBLKS EQU   *
         MVC   0(TUALNG09,R6),TUALLO09 SET DEFAULT BLOCK LENGTH
         CLC   R99BLKL,ZEROAMT         BLOCK LENGTH SUPPLIED?
         BC    9,*+14                  NO, USE OUR DEFAULT
         MVC   7(2,R6),R99BLKL         USE SUPPLIED BLOCK LENGTH
         BC    15,*+20                 BYPASS ADDITIONAL CHECKING
         CLC   R99BLKSZ,ZEROAMT        BLOCKSIZE 0 AS WELL?

         MVC   7(2,R6),R99BLKSZ        USE BLOCKSIZE FOR LENGTH
         LA    R6,TUALNG09(R6)         POINT TO NEXT TU FIELD

CHKDSORG EQU   *
         TM    R99DSORG,R99DSGSP       DSORG SUPPLIED?
         BC    8,CHKBLKSZ              NO, GO CHECK FOR BLOCKSIZE
         LA    R5,S99TUPL+4            GET ADDRESS OF NEXT TU PTR
         ST    R6,S99TUPTR             SAVE NXT ADDR IN TU PTR LIST
         MVC   0(TUALNG3C,R6),TUALLO3C SET FOR A PDS
         TM    R99DSORG,R99PDS         IS THIS A NEW PDS?
         BC    8,*+12                  NO, GO CHECK ANOTHER
         LA    R6,TUALNG3C(R6)         POINT TO NEXT TU FIELD
         BC    15,CHKBLKSZ             GO CHECK BLKSIZE
         TM    R99DSORG,R99VSAM        IS THIS A NEW VSAM FILE?
         BC    8,*+18                  NO, GO CHECK ANOTHER
         MVC   6(2,R6),S99DVSAM        SAY DSORG IS VSAM
         LA    R6,TUALNG3C(R6)         POINT TO NEXT TU FIELD
         BC    15,CHKBLKSZ             GO CHECK BLKSIZE
         TM    R99DSORG,R99DA          IS THIS A NEW DA FILE?
         BC    8,*+18                  NO, GO CHECK ANOTHER
         MVC   6(2,R6),S99DDA          SAY DSORG IS DA
         LA    R6,TUALNG3C(R6)         POINT TO NEXT TU FIELD
         BC    15,CHKBLKSZ             GO CHECK BLKSIZE
         TM    R99DSORG,R99PS          IS THIS A NEW PS FILE?
         BC    8,CHKBLKSZ              NO, GO CHECK BLKSIZE
         MVC   6(2,R6),S99DPS          SAY DSORG IS PS

*******************************************************************
CHKEXPIR EQU   *
         TM    R99EXPR,255-C' '  NON-NULL, NON-BLANK?           GP98108
         BZ    CHKRETN       NEITHER; NO EXPIRATION GIVEN       GP98108
         LA    R5,S99TUPL+4            GET ADDRESS OF NEXT TU PTR
         ST    R6,S99TUPTR             SAVE EXPIR. TU PTR LIST
         MVC   0(TUALNG22,R6),TUALLO22 SET MEMBER TU FIXED PORTION
*  NOTE:  THIS CODE GENERATES A NEW FORMAT (LONG) YYYYDDD DATE. GP98108
*    THE NEXT MOVE WILL USE A 19 FOR THE CENTURY UNTIL THE      GP98108
*    R99EXPR FIELD IS EXPANDED (AND DATA ARE FILLED IN!)        GP98108
         MVC   6+L'TUTX22-L'R99EXPR(L'R99EXPR,R6),R99EXPR       GP98108
         LA    R6,TUALNG22(R6)         POINT TO LENGTH TU LNG FIELD
         BC    15,CHKKEYL              GO CHECK FOR KEYLENGTH

UNALLRTN EQU   *
         TM    R99PRCSS,R99UNALL       UNALLOCATION REQUESTED
         BC    8,CONCTRTN              NO, GO CHECK CONCATENATION
         SPACE 2
*******************************************************************
*            DATASET UNALLOCATION SECTION BEGINS HERE
*******************************************************************
         MVI   S99VERB,S99VRBUN        SET FOR DYNAMIC UNALLOCATION
         SPACE
         MVC   0(TUDLNG07,R6),TUDEAL07 SET TO UNALLOCATE DATASET
         LA    R6,TUALNG07(R6)         POINT TO NEXT TU FIELD
         SPACE
         TM    R99DDNAM,255-C' ' DDNAME PRESENT?                GP98108
         BZ    CHKDSNUN          NO, GO CHECK FOR DSNAME        GP98108
         SPACE 2
*******************************************************************
*      DDNAME TEXT UNIT BUILD AREA
*******************************************************************
         LA    R5,S99TUPL+4            GET ADDRESS OF NEXT TU PTR
         ST    R6,S99TUPTR             SAVE NXT ADDR IN TU PTR LIST
         MVC   0(TUDLNG01,R6),TUDEAL01 SET DDNAME TU FIXED PORTION
         LA    R6,TUDLNG01(R6)         POINT TO LENGTH TU LNG FIELD
         LA    R15,R99DDNAM            LOAD ADDRESS OF DDNAME
         LA    R14,8                   LOAD FULL FIELD LENGTH
         BAL   R9,FINDLNG              GO FIND FIELD LENGTH
         BC    15,CHKOVRD              GO CHECK FOR OVERRIDE
         SPACE 2
*******************************************************************
*      DSNAME TEXT UNIT BUILD AREA
*******************************************************************
CHKDSNUN EQU   *
         TM    R99DSN,255-C' '   DSNAME PRESENT?                GP98108
         BZ    CHKOVRD           NO, GO CHECK FOR OVERRIDE      GP98108
         LA    R5,S99TUPL+4            GET ADDRESS OF NEXT TU PTR
         ST    R6,S99TUPTR             SAVE NXT ADDR IN TU PTR LIST
         MVC   0(TUDLNG02,R6),TUDEAL02 SET DSNAME TU FIXED PORTION
         LA    R6,TUDLNG02(R6)         POINT TO LENGTH TU LNG FIELD
         LA    15,R99DSN               LOAD ADDRESS OF DDNAME
         LA    R14,44                  LOAD FULL FIELD LENGTH
         BAL   R9,FINDLNG              GO FIND FIELD LENGTH
         SPACE 2
*******************************************************************
*      MEMBER TEXT UNIT BUILD AREA
*******************************************************************
         TM    R99MEMBR,255-C' ' MEMBER NAME PRESENT?           GP98108
         BZ    CHKOVRD           NO, GO CHECK FOR OVERRIDE      GP98108
         LA    R5,S99TUPL+4            GET ADDRESS OF NEXT TU PTR
         ST    R6,S99TUPTR             SAVE NXT ADDR IN TU PTR LIST
         MVC   0(TUDLNG03,R6),TUDEAL03 SET MEMBER TU FIXED PORTION
         LA    R6,TUDLNG03(R6)         POINT TO LENGTH TU LNG FIELD
         LA    15,R99MEMBR             LOAD ADDRESS OF MEMBER
         LA    R14,8                   LOAD FULL FIELD LENGTH
         BAL   R9,FINDLNG              GO FIND FIELD LENGTH
         SPACE 2
*******************************************************************
*      DISPOSTION OVERRIDE TEXT UNIT BUILD AREA
*******************************************************************
CHKOVRD  EQU   *
         TM    R99STATS,R99OVRD        OVERRIDING DISPOSITION?
         BC    8,ISSUEIT               NO, GO ISSUE SVC99 CALL
         LA    R5,S99TUPL+4            GET ADDRESS OF NEXT TU PTR
         ST    R6,S99TUPTR             SAVE NXT ADDR IN TU PTR LIST
         MVC   0(TUDLNG05,R6),TUDEAL05 SET OVERRIDE DISPOSTION
         TM    R99NDISP,R99DSSUP       DISPOSITION SUPPLIED?
         BC    8,*+14                  NO, USE THE DEFAULT
         MVC   6(1,R6),R99NDISP        MOVE REQUESTED DISP TO TU
         NI    6(R6),RLYHEX0F          REMOVE EXTRANEOUS INFORMATION
         LA    R6,TUDLNG05(R6)         POINT TO NEXT TU FIELD
         BC    15,ISSUEIT              GO ISSUE SVC99 CALL
         SPACE
CONCTRTN EQU   *
         TM    R99PRCSS,R99CNCT        CONCATENATION REQUESTED
         BC    8,DCNCTRTN              NO, GO CHECK CONCATENATION
         SPACE 2
*******************************************************************
*            DATASET CONCATENATION SECTION BEGINS HERE
*******************************************************************
         MVI   S99VERB,S99VRBCC        SET FOR DYNAMIC CONCATENATION
         SPACE 2
*******************************************************************
*      CONCATENATION DDNAME TEXT UNIT BUILD AREA - DDNAME #1
*******************************************************************
         MVC   0(TUCLNG01,R6),TUCONC01 SET CONCAT. TU FIXED PORTION
         ST    R6,R99TUPSV             SAVE TEXT UNIT POSITION
         LA    R6,TUCLNG01(R6)         POINT TO LENGTH TU LNG FIELD
         LA    15,R99CNCT1             LOAD ADDRESS OF DDNAME #1
         LA    R14,8                   LOAD FULL FIELD LENGTH
         BAL   R9,FINDLNG              GO FIND FIELD LENGTH
         SPACE 2
*******************************************************************
*      CONCATENATION DDNAME TEXT UNIT BUILD AREA - DDNAME #2
*******************************************************************
         LA    15,R99CNCT2             LOAD ADDRESS OF DDNAME #2
         LA    R14,8                   LOAD FULL FIELD LENGTH
         BAL   R9,FINDLNG              GO FIND FIELD LENGTH
         SPACE 2
*******************************************************************
*      CONCATENATION DDNAME TEXT UNIT BUILD AREA - DDNAME #3
*******************************************************************
CHKFDDN3 EQU   *
         TM    R99CNCT3,255-C' ' VOLSER #3 SPECIFIED?           GP98108
         BZ    ISSUEIT           NO, GO ISSUE SVC99 CALL        GP98108
         CLI   R99CNCT3,BLNK           VOLSER #3 SPECIFIED?
         BC    9,ISSUEIT               NO, GO ISSUE SVC99 CALL
         L     R15,R99TUPSV            RELOAD TEXT UNIT POSITION
         MVI   3(R15),RLYHEX03         SET NUMBER DDNAMES TO 3
         LA    15,R99CNCT3             LOAD ADDRESS OF DDNAME #3
         LA    R14,8                   LOAD FULL FIELD LENGTH
         BAL   R9,FINDLNG              GO FIND FIELD LENGTH
         SPACE 2
*******************************************************************
*      CONCATENATION DDNAME TEXT UNIT BUILD AREA - DDNAME #4
*******************************************************************
         TM    R99CNCT4,255-C' ' VOLSER #4 SPECIFIED?           GP98108
         BZ    ISSUEIT           NO, GO ISSUE SVC99 CALL        GP98108
         L     R15,R99TUPSV            RELOAD TEXT UNIT POSITION
         MVI   3(R15),RLYHEX04         SET NUMBER DDNAMES TO 4
         LA    15,R99CNCT4             LOAD ADDRESS OF DDNAME #4
         LA    R14,8                   LOAD FULL FIELD LENGTH
         BAL   R9,FINDLNG              GO FIND FIELD LENGTH
         SPACE 2
*******************************************************************
*      CONCATENATION DDNAME TEXT UNIT BUILD AREA - DDNAME #5
*******************************************************************
         TM    R99CNCT5,255-C' ' VOLSER #5 SPECIFIED?           GP98108
         BZ    ISSUEIT           NO, GO ISSUE SVC99 CALL        GP98108
         L     R15,R99TUPSV            RELOAD TEXT UNIT POSITION
         MVI   3(R15),RLYHEX05         SET NUMBER DDNAMES TO 5
         LA    15,R99CNCT5             LOAD ADDRESS OF DDNAME #5
         LA    R14,8                   LOAD FULL FIELD LENGTH
         BAL   R9,FINDLNG              GO FIND FIELD LENGTH
         BC    15,ISSUEIT              GO ISSUE SVC99 CALL
         SPACE
DCNCTRTN EQU   *
         TM    R99PRCSS,R99DCAT        DECONCATENATION REQUESTED
         BC    8,ALLDAX4               NO, THERE'S AN ERROR HERE
         SPACE 2
*******************************************************************
*           DATASET DECONCATENATION SECTION BEGINS HERE
*******************************************************************
         MVI   S99VERB,S99VRBDC        SET FOR DYNAM DECONCATENATION
         SPACE 2
*******************************************************************
*      DECONCATENATION DDNAME TEXT UNIT BUILD AREA
*******************************************************************
         MVC   0(TUDCLN01,R6),TUDCON01 SET DDNAME TU FIXED PORTION
         LA    R6,TUDCLN01(R6)         POINT TO LENGTH TU LNG FIELD
         LA    R15,R99DDNAM            LOAD ADDRESS OF DDNAME
         LA    R14,8                   LOAD FULL FIELD LENGTH
         BAL   R9,FINDLNG              GO FIND FIELD LENGTH
         BC    15,ISSUEIT              GO ISSUE SVC99 CALL
         SPACE 2
*******************************************************************
*
*       ISUUE DYNALLOC MACRO HERE (SVC99 CALL)
*
*******************************************************************
ISSUEIT  EQU   *
         OI    S99TUPTR,S99TUPLN       TAINT HIGH ORDER BIT
         LR    R1,R3                   LOAD REQUEST BLOCK PTR ADDRESS
         SPACE
         DYNALLOC
         SPACE 2
*******************************************************************
*      RETURN SVC99 RETURN INFORMATION TO CALLER
*******************************************************************
         MVC   R99ERRCD,S99ERROR       RETURN ERROR CODE FIELD
         MVC   R99INFCD,S99INFO        RETURN INFORMATION CODE FIELD
         CLC   R99ERRCD,=X'0000'       ANY ERRORS?
         BC    7,ALLDAX4               YES, GO NOTIFY THE USER
         SPACE
         TM    R99AFLG1,R99SYSOT       SYSOUT DATASET?
         BC    1,RTRNDSRG              YES, ONLY RETURN DSORG
         SPACE
         L     R15,R99VOLAD            POINT TO VOLSER PARM FIELD
         MVC   R99VOLS1(6),0(R15)      RETURN VOLSER TO USER
         SPACE
RTRNDSRG EQU   *
         L     R15,R99DSGAD            POINT TO DSORG PARM FIELD
         ICM   R0,3,0(R15)   LOAD DSORG BITS FOR FASTER CHECK   GP97253
         N     R0,=X'0000FEFF'  AND MASKING - KILL UNMOVABLE    GP97253
         SPACE
         CLM   R0,3,=X'0200'           PO DSORG?                GP97253
         BC    7,*+12                  NO, GO CHECK NEXT DSORG
         OI    R99DSORG,R99PDS         TELL USER THIS IS A PDS
         BC    15,LNKS99EX             GO RETURN
         SPACE
         TM    1(R15),X'08'            VSAM DSORG?              GP98297
         BZ    *+12                    NO, GO CHECK NEXT DSORG  GP98297
         OI    R99DSORG,R99VSAM        TELL USER THIS IS VSAM
         BC    15,LNKS99EX             GO RETURN
         SPACE
         CLM   R0,3,=X'2000'           DA DSORG?                GP97253
         BC    7,*+12                  NO, GO CHECK NEXT DSORG
         OI    R99DSORG,R99DA          TELL USER THIS IS DA
         BC    15,LNKS99EX             GO RETURN
         SPACE
         CLM   R0,3,=X'4000'           PS DSORG?                GP97253
         BC    7,LNKS99EX              NO, JUST GO RETURN
         OI    R99DSORG,R99PS          TELL USER THIS IS PS
         SPACE 2
********************************************************************
*        RETURN TO OUR CALLER
********************************************************************
LNKS99EX EQU   *                       ALL FINISHED HERE:
         RETURN RC=0                   RETURN TO OUR CALLER
         SPACE  4
ALLDAX4  EQU   *                       FILE ALLOCATION ERROR:
         RETURN RC=8                   RETURN TO OUR CALLER
         EJECT
********************************************************************
*
*        SUBROUTINE TO FIND TRUE INPUT PARAMETER LENGTH
*
********************************************************************
FINDLNG  EQU   *
         XR    R1,R1                   CLEAR WORK REGISTER
         ST    R15,R99ADDSV            SAVE INPUT PARM ADDRESS
RTNCOMP  EQU   *
         TM    0(R15),255-C' '   END OF VALID ITEM?             GP98108
         BZ    MOVEDAT           YES, GO MOVE THE DATA          GP98108
         LA    R15,1(R15)              POINT UP TO NEXT INPUT BYTE
         LA    R1,1(R1)                INCREMENT MOVE LENGTH
         BCT   R14,RTNCOMP             GO BACK UNTIL LENGTH FOUND
MOVEDAT  EQU   *
         STCM  R1,B'0011',0(R6)        SAVE LENGTH FOR THIS TU
         LA    R6,2(R6)                POINT PAST LENGTH FIELD
         L     R15,R99ADDSV            RELOAD INPUT PARM ADDRESS
         BCT   R1,*+4                  LESS 1 FOR THE MOVE
         EX    R1,MOVEPARM             MOVE IT
         LA    R1,1(R1)                RESTORE ORIGINAL LENGTH
         AR    R6,R1                   POINT PAST PARM FIELD
         BR    R9                      RETURN TO OUR CALLER
         SPACE 4
MOVEPARM MVC   0(1,R6),0(R15)          EXECUTE IT
         EJECT

S99DPS   DC    XL2'4000'

***********************************************************************
* THIS IS A TYPICAL TSSO PARAMETER DECK FOR A TYPICAL SYSTEM. THE     *
* DOCUMENTATION IS   IN "TSSO SYSTEM PROGRAMMERS GUIDE- RELEASE 4.3   *
* THESE VALUES SHOULD WORK AS DEFAULTS.                               *
* NOTE THAT THE ONLY NEW PARAMETER IN TSSO 4.3 IS THE NUMCONS PARM.   *
***********************************************************************
NONSWAP=Y
************************************************************
* TSSO WILL BE RUNNING NON-SWAPPABLE                       *
************************************************************
*
TABLE=AOFIVP
************************************************************
* THE TABLE NAME FOR TSSO AOF WILL BE AOFIVP               *
************************************************************
*
RACFID=IBMUSER
************************************************************
* TSSO WILL ASSUME A RACF USERID OF "TSSO" ON STARTUP      *
************************************************************
*
SRC=#
************************************************************
* THE COMMAND RECOGNITION CHARACTER IS A POUND SIGN ('#')  *
************************************************************
*
MAXCMDS=15
************************************************************
* TSSO WILL HANDLE AT MOST 15 SIMULTANEOUS COMMANDS        *
************************************************************
*
MAXWTO=250
************************************************************
* TSSO WILL ISSUE AT MOST 250 WTOS FOR ANY ONE COMMAND     *
************************************************************
*
PROMPT=NO
************************************************************
* DO NOT PROMPT THE MVS OPERATOR FOR ADDITIONAL TSSO       *
* PARAMETERS                                               *
************************************************************
*
SECSYS=RACF
***********************************************************************
* THE SECURITY SYSTEM IN USE WILL BE THE RESOURCE ACCESS CONTROL      *
* FACILITY.                                                           *
***********************************************************************
*
SECLEVEL=MINIMAL
***********************************************************************
* WE WILL BE USING THE "MINIMAL" LEVEL OF SECURITY, SO YOU CAN PHASE  *
* IN CONSOLE SECURITY AT A LATER DATE.                                *
***********************************************************************
*
SUBSYS 9 = TSSOSS09
***********************************************************************
* THE "TSSOSS09" ROUTINE, SUPPLIED WITH TSSO, WILL BE PROCESSING      *
* THE WTO AND WTOR MESSAGES WHEN AOF IS ACTIVE. ANY OTHER SELECTION   *
* MAY CAUSE TSSO TO FAIL.                                             *
***********************************************************************
*
SUBSYS 10 = TSSOSS10
***********************************************************************
* THE "TSSOSS10" ROUTINE, SUPPLIED WITH TSSO, WILL BE PROCESSING      *
* THE MVS AND SUBSYSTEM COMMANDS. ANY OTHER SELECTION MAY MAKE TSSO   *
* FAIL.                                                               *
***********************************************************************
*
TIMEOUT = 30
***********************************************************************
* IF THE SECLEVEL PARAMETER IS EVER SET TO "MAX", CONSOLES WILL TIME  *
* OUT AFTER THIRTY MINUTES OF INACTIVITY...                           *
***********************************************************************
*
NUMCONS = 10 DEDICATE
***********************************************************************
* TSSO WILL HAVE 10 SUBSYSTEM CONSOLES AT ITS DISPOSAL. ONE OF THESE  *
* CONSOLES WILL BE DEDICATED TO THE TSSO ADDRESS SPACE.               *
***********************************************************************
END

./ ADD NAME=WYLBCMDA,SSI=00092260
;
;    OBS WYLBUR/MILTEN REL 8.1 STARTUP COMMANDS         9/92
;        FOR X/A SYSTEM A
;
;    3 OF 3 (FOLLOWS WYLBINIT, WYLBLINA)
;
;    SYSTEM INITIALIZATION COMMANDS
;
DEFSYS WYLBUR ALL                  ; WYLBUR IS DEFAULT SUBSYSTEM
SET RMF OFF                        ; SET ON AFTER RMF START
BEGIN WYLRCVY WAIT ABEND=DUMP      ; WAIT FOR RECOVERY TASK
BEGIN WYLBUR ABEND=DUMP
;
;ET WORD MILTEN PRESTO             ;
;
ATTACH ALL                         ; ATTACH ALL COMPONENTS
START  ALL                         ; START ALL ATTACHED COMPONENTS
OPEN VTAM APPLID=WYLBUR            ; OPEN WYLBUR TEST VTAM APPL
;
;BEGIN TSO SYNC                     ; IF WE EVER GET PASS-THROUGH
;CALL TSO SET APPLROOT=TSWY         ; APPL NAME PREFIX
;CALL TSO SET MAXSESS=10            ; MORE THAN NECESSARY ?
;
;BEGIN CICS SYNC                    ; A-SYSTEM ONLY
;CALL CICS SET APPLROOT=Y           ; APPL NAME PREFIX
;CALL CICS SET MAXSESS=4            ; IN-HOUSE ONLY
;
SET WTRACE OFF                     ; ON ONLY IN DEBUG VERSION
SET CPULIM ON MON=10 INT=.5 PC=10  ; LIMIT CPU HOGGING
;                                                                92260
;                                                                92260
 BEGIN WYLKERM                      ; ENABLE KERMIT FILE TRANSFER
;                                                                92260
;                                                                92260

./ ADD NAME=WYLBINIT,SSI=00092260
;
;    OBS WYLBUR/MILTEN REL 8.1 BASIC INITIALIZATION          9/92
;        FOR X/A SYSTEM A
;
;    TERMINAL GREETING MESSAGE (0-45 BYTES)
;
INIT INSTALN='Public Interest Data, Inc. - X/A Wylbur 8.1'
;
;
;    SYSTEM CONSOLE DEFINITIONS
;
INIT CONSOLE=UTILCONS TYPE=SYSTEM-CONSOLE ID=255 UID=SYSTEMS  ;
INIT CONSOLE=CONS1    TYPE=3277-2-CONSOLE ID=01  UID=OPERATR  ;
INIT CONSOLE=CONS2    TYPE=3277-2-CONSOLE ID=02  UID=OPERCRT  ;
INIT CONSOLE=CONS3    TYPE=3277-2-CONSOLE ID=03  UID=OPERCRT  ;
;
INIT XTRASYS 4                   ; STARTABLE SUB-SYSTEMS
INIT DYNAMNET=64                 ;UP TO 64 CONCURRENT VTAM SESSIONS
INIT CDWAIT 9                    ;WAIT 9 SEC FOR SIGNOFF MSGS
INIT MODE SPKA                     ; RUN IN SUPVSR STATE
;

BEGIN WYLRCVY WAIT ABEND=DUMP      ; WAIT FOR RECOVERY TASK
BEGIN WYLBUR SYNC ABEND=DUMP
;
SET WORD MILTEN SYSTEMS            ; >>>>> SYSTEMS ONLY <<<<<    93158
;
ATTACH ALL                         ; ATTACH ALL COMPONENTS
START  ALL                         ; START ALL ATTACHED COMPONENTS
OPEN VTAM APPLID=WYLBUR            ; OPEN WYLBUR TEST VTAM APPL
;
;BEGIN TSO SYNC                     ; IF WE EVER GET PASS-THROUGH

;
;
SET FAILSOFT ON                    ;ENABLE FAILSOFT RECOVERY
;
;
;
